### 1. 美食银河：宇宙级印度街头小吃太阳系

**作者**: [Ashish Sheth](https://x.com/commanderdgr8/status/2039908503058305284)  **日期**: 2026-04-03  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana 2 设计的创意且详尽的提示词，旨在生成一张超现实、照片级真实的图像，展现漂浮在深空中的印度街头小吃。每种食物都代表一个天体（例如：坦都里烤饼作为太阳，脆球饼作为行星，咖喱角作为小行星）。提示词详细说明了光影、背景元素（香料星云、拉西银河）及艺术风格。

![美食银河：宇宙级印度街头小吃太阳系](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284657172_qor3qr_HE81-SpWAAAmvxM.jpg)

```
Create a cosmic/space scene where various Indian street foods are floating in deep space as if they are planets, moons, and celestial objects in a delicious galaxy.

THE FOOD SOLAR SYSTEM:
- CENTER (Sun): A massive round tandoori roti, glowing from within like a star, with charred spots resembling sunspots, radiating warm golden light outward
- PLANET 1 (closest): A perfect round golgappa/pani puri — crispy shell glistening, filled with spiced water visible through the opening. Tiny orbit ring of sev and chutney droplets.
- PLANET 2: A round vada (medu vada) as a donut-shaped planet with a ring system made of coconut chutney
- PLANET 3: A plate of round gulab jamuns as a cluster of sweet brown planets with syrup nebula around them
- ASTEROID BELT: Dozens of floating samosas, pakoras, and bhel pieces scattered in a ring
- PLANET 4 (gas giant): A huge round dahi vada — white yogurt surface like a cloudy gas giant, with tempering (tadka) marks resembling Jupiter's storms
- COMET: A kebab skewer streaking across the scene with a trail of spice smoke and sparks
- MOON: A round idli orbiting the dahi vada planet
- NEBULA: A colorful cloud of turmeric (yellow), chili (red), and coriander (green) powders mixing in space, forming a stunning spice nebula

BACKGROUND:
- Deep space black with thousands of tiny stars (mustard seeds and cumin seeds floating as stars)
- Distant galaxies made of swirling masala powder
- The Milky Way visible but made of a stream of white lassi/buttermilk

LIGHTING:
- The tandoori roti "sun" provides warm orange light illuminating nearby foods
- Each food item has its own subtle glow — the hot items emit warm light, the cold items (lassi, curd) emit cool blue light
- Dramatic space lighting: stark bright highlights, deep black shadows, no atmosphere

STYLE: Photorealistic food photography meets NASA space photography. Every food item is rendered with appetite-triggering detail — crispy textures, steam, glistening oil, fresh garnishes — but floating in actual outer space with real stars and cosmic phenomena. This surreal combination is the kind of image people share saying "this is the most Indian thing I've ever seen." 8K resolution.
```

**Related**: [[超现实]]、[[综合奇幻]]、[[美食摄影]]

### 2. 动态波普艺术视频序列

**作者**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto/status/2039659110124200243)  **日期**: 2026-04-02  **语言**: ja

> 该提示词用于在 Nano Banana Pro 中生成单场景图像（包含模特），随后使用 Kling 3.0 Omni 创建了 5 镜头的视频序列。提示词描述了一个充满活力、动感十足的视频序列，主角是一位身着波普艺术风格服装的金发女性，背景为色彩斑斓的街道。

![动态波普艺术视频序列](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775198518238_qpcd0k_HE3SS2ZboAAcmXt.jpg)

```
晴れたカラフルなストリートで躍動する、白いチューブトップとピンクのミニスカート、厚底スニーカーを身に着けた金髪ボブの女性モデル。足元からのティルトアップに始まり、ポップアート前でのキュートなウインク、笑顔でスキップするローアングルの並走ショット、シャボン玉を吹くハイアングルの旋回ショットを経て、最後はターンしてハートポーズを決める姿から青空へと一気にプルバックする。アップテンポなポップミュージックと魔法のような効果音がシンクロする、ダイナミックでエネルギッシュな映像。
```

### 3. 由切片果蔬重构的角色

**作者**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_/status/2039431574916104474)  **日期**: 2026-04-01  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示词，旨在将上传的角色参考图转换为完全由层叠、切片果蔬构成的逼真 3D 渲染图。在确保所有材质（包括鞋履）均由果蔬切片构成的前提下，精准保留原角色的比例、色彩和特征。

![由切片果蔬重构的角色](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112279816_ougqwk_HE2DyO3WwAAhQtr.jpg)

```
create a version of this character made entirely of sliced vegetables and fruits vegetables and fruits: should match the uploaded character’s colors as closely as possible, without changing their natural look slices: slightly misaligned, with visible separation between layers structure: a small bite taken out of the top of the head, forming a clean cut surface ambience: kitchen setting, on a cutting board with scattered vegetables and a knife nearby camera: slightly top-down angle effect: tilt-shift  Likeness Preservation (CRITICAL): Maintain exact proportions, eye shape, spacing, stylization, silhouette, and material identity from the reference Do not humanize Do not reinterpret anatomy Do not modify facial structure Identity must remain perfectly intact and instantly recognizable Character Compatibility Rules: If the uploaded character is 2D, convert it into a believable realistic 3D render while preserving the original design, proportions, colors, and visual identity Do not modify facial structure  Do not add a mouth or nose if the uploaded character does not have them  👟 FOOTWEAR & ACCESSORY MATERIAL OVERRIDE (CRITICAL FIX) All parts of the character, including footwear and clothing, must follow the same fruit and vegetable slice construction. • shoes must be made entirely of stacked fruit and vegetable slices  • preserve the exact shoe shape, proportions, and design  • recreate panels, sole, and details using layered slices Material examples for shoes: • sole → dense stacked potato or root vegetable slices  • upper panels → fruit/vegetable slices arranged to match original color blocking  • edges and seams → visible slice layering and separation 📷⚠️ 0px; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: 2; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; widows: 2; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;"> IMPORTANT:  No original materials should remain (no fabric, rubber, or leather).  Everything must be converted into fruit/vegetable slice construction while keeping the original design recognizable. ar 1:1
```

**Related**: [[微缩模型与立体模型]]、[[3D渲染]]、[[综合3D]]

### 4. 动态波普艺术街景视频提示词

**作者**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto/status/2039251418507542544)  **日期**: 2026-04-01  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个详细的多镜头提示词，适用于图像生成（Nano Banana Pro）和后续的视频生成（Kling 3.0 Omni）。它描述了一个充满活力、动感十足的视频序列，主角是一位留着金色波波头的女性模特，身着波普艺术风格服装，在阳光明媚、色彩斑斓的街道上进行各种动作，并与快节奏的流行音乐同步。

```
晴れたカラフルなストリートで躍動する、白いチューブトップとピンクのミニスカート、厚底スニーカーを身に着けた金髪ボブの女性モデル。足元からのティルトアップに始まり、ポップアート前でのキュートなウインク、笑顔でスキップするローアングルの並走ショット、シャボン玉を吹くハイアングルの旋回ショットを経て、最後はターンしてハートポーズを決める姿から青空へと一気にプルバックする。アップテンポなポップミュージックと魔法のような効果音がシンクロする、ダイナミックでエネルギッシュな映像。
```

### 5. 参考角色姿势网格研究提示词

**作者**: [Echo Callers](https://x.com/echocallers/status/2039037202684842107)  **日期**: 2026-03-31  **语言**: en

> 这是一份为 nano banana 编写的详细提示词，旨在生成 2x3 网格视角的参考角色研究图，通过从极远景到极特写的六个特定分镜，专注于保持角色的一致性并根据镜头距离调整姿势。

![参考角色姿势网格研究提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775026353345_nztfg3_HEwdhneWkAA2At1.jpg)

```
16:9 landscape, 2x3 grid perspective study of the reference character on a solid off-white background. 6 panels in strict order: 1. Extreme Wide (silhouette focus), 2. Full Body (dynamic pose), 3. Waist-Up (torso twist), 4. Bust Shot (strong posture), 5. Face Close-Up (expression), 6. Extreme Close-Up (facial details/eyes).
- Consistency: Maintain identical facial structure, hair, and proportions across all panels.
- Posing: Tailor gestures to camera distance—broad movements for wide shots, subtle nuances for close-ups.
- Aesthetic: Consistent lighting and art style; no borders, text, or background environments.
```
---

### 7. 肖邦《幻想即兴曲》的 Lassen 风格演绎

**作者**: [クラリネットクラリオンNOBU](https://x.com/NOBU79834619/status/2038200741652021680)  **日期**: 2026-03-29  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个与 Nano Banana Pro (Gemini 3 Pro Image) 配合使用的提示词，旨在根据肖邦的《幻想即兴曲》(Op. 66) 生成图像，并以 Christian Riese Lassen 的艺术风格进行渲染，最终呈现出一幅以海豚和虎鲸为主角，而非人物的场景。

![肖邦《幻想即兴曲》的 Lassen 风格演绎](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853754094_liae34_HEkkxDUbMAAYaCb.jpg)

```
ショパン

幻想即興曲　作品66のイメージ
ラッセン風味

その時　人はいなくなり

イルカとシャチは現れた？
```

### 8. 适用于 Nano Banana 2 的极繁主义谷物艺术提示词

**作者**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp/status/2037816970784264510)  **日期**: 2026-03-28  **语言**: ja

> 这是一份为 Nano Banana 2 编写的详细提示词，旨在生成一幅极繁主义杰作。该作品采用享誉全球的谷物艺术家周志江的风格，描绘了五种谷物，其排列方式参考了示例图像，背景为黄色小米，强调高分辨率与精细细节。

![适用于 Nano Banana 2 的极繁主义谷物艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774766205832_1e2zsf_HEavoUVb0AA5kjn.jpg)
![适用于 Nano Banana 2 的极繁主义谷物艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774766205826_68ikix_HEavo40bIAAxwcE.jpg)

```
世界的に有名な穀物画の巨匠、周志江による、マキシマリスト様式の傑作。黄色い粟を背景に、5粒の穀物が参考画像のように配置されています。穀物本来の色合いと、その配置によって生み出される立体感が、絵画をより一層生き生きとさせています。高解像度、精緻な描写、超高精細、最高品質。
```

### 12. 超详细的 Sabrina Carpenter 图像生成 JSON 提示词

**作者**: [Pinodi](https://x.com/PinodiArt/status/2034252141963923471)  **日期**: 2026-03-18  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示词，专为 Nano Banana Pro 设计，用于生成 Sabrina Carpenter 的图像。该提示词指定了生物特征细节、服装（白色连体裤，红色配饰）、姿势（在厨房台面上眨眼）、场景（20 世纪 70 年代复古厨房），以及精确的灯光和物理设置，以实现超现实的输出效果。

![超详细的 Sabrina Carpenter 图像生成 JSON 提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773902671302_pg1nzd_HDsdcrVaUAAonxw.jpg)
![超详细的 Sabrina Carpenter 图像生成 JSON 提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773902671404_afh40i_HDsdea6XkAAVfbP.jpg)
![超详细的 Sabrina Carpenter 图像生成 JSON 提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773902671519_qdflv9_HDsdbOkWEAA3jGN.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "identity": {
      "biometric_reference": "{argument name="biometric reference" default="Sabrina Carpenter"}",
      "facial_biometry": {
        "structure": "Heart-shaped facial morphology, defined zygomatic arches, soft jawline with subtle mentalis definition",
        "eyes": "Almond-shaped orbits, sapphire blue iris stroma with distinct radial patterns and limbal rings, long natural eyelashes",
        "nose": "Refined dorsum, slightly upturned nasal tip, symmetrical alar base",
        "mouth": "Pronounced cupid's bow, specific vermilion border, orthodontic-grade teeth alignment with natural incisor translucency during a wink expression",
        "hair": "{argument name="hair color" default="Honey blonde #E3C58D"}, voluminous waves in high pigtails, thick curtain bangs, silk texture with micro-strand detail"
      }
    },
    "body": {
      "somatotype": "Petite hourglass mesomorph, precise 0.7 waist-to-hip ratio",
      "skin": {
        "tone": "Warm ivory hex #FFF5EE",
        "physics": "Subsurface scattering enabled, realistic epidermal micro-texture, zero beautify smoothing, visible natural skin pores",
        "details": "Soft clavicle definition, natural knee-cap anatomy, accurate foot morphology without digital artifacts"
      }
    }
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top_piece": "Off-the-shoulder white #FFFFFF cotton-spandex romper, elasticated puff sleeves, centered red #D2122E silk ribbon bow",
    "legwear": "Opaque white #FFFFFF knee-high cotton socks, matte texture",
    "footwear": "Glossy red #B22222 Mary Jane platform heels, double ankle straps with silver buckles",
    "accessories": "Red #D2122E velvet hair ribbons, matching thin red choker with a small metallic pendant"
  },
  "pose_action": {
    "primary_pose": "Sitting on a kitchen countertop, right leg extended, left leg slightly bent, leaning on right arm for support",
    "expression": "Playful wink with right eye closed, authentic nasolabial fold activation, natural smile showing upper dentition",
    "interaction": "Left hand holding a small vintage-style snack package, fingers articulated with anatomically correct joints"
  },
  "scene": {
    "environment": "1970s retro-aesthetic kitchen",
    "background_elements": {
      "wall": "Off-white matte finish with vintage Japanese-style city-pop posters and magazine clippings",
      "backsplash": "Checkered sage green #9CB08D and cream #F5F5DC square ceramic tiles, realistic grout lines",
      "countertop": "White marble texture with subtle grey veining",
      "props": "Vintage beige record player with a rotating black vinyl disc, red aluminum cans #EE1C25, scattered yellow and red snack bags"
    },
    "cabinetry": "Muted sage green #A9BA9D lower cabinets with polished chrome handles, integrated retro oven unit"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "setup": "Soft-box studio lighting mimicking 70s film photography, warm color temperature",
    "physics": "Accurate specular highlights on glossy sur"
  }
}
```

### 26. 夏洛克·福尔摩斯华丽橱柜立体模型提示

**作者**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent/status/2028465420756475917)  **日期**: 2026-03-02  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂、结构化的提示模板，用于 Nano Banana 2 生成一个华丽橱柜立体模型的超现实渲染图。该立体模型必须包含三个架子，每个架子都描绘了《福尔摩斯历险记》中的一个场景。该提示使用可变指南来控制材料、风格、照明和摄像机角度，并对构图和结构提供了严格的指示（必须是开放式正面，无门）。

![夏洛克·福尔摩斯华丽橱柜立体模型提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772519728539_psugzr_HCaOVaEasAAR2n7.jpg)

```
Variable Guide
1. OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME = Scenes from Adventures of Sherlock Holmes by Arthur Conan Doyle, in the order in which they are presented in the book
2. CUPBOARD_BASE_MATERIAL = 
3. CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL = 
4. RACK_MATERIAL = 
5. ORNAMENTATION_STYLE = [e.g., Gothic carved wood, Art Deco brass, Elven interlaced vines]
6. ART_STYLE = Hyper-Realistic Render
7. TOP_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
8. MIDDLE_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
9. BOTTOM_SHELF_SCENE = [Describe specific actions of miniature figures defining the scene]
10. LIGHTING = 
11. CAMERA_ANGLE = A straight-on, front-facing view, captured from a moderately high angle looking distinctly downward.
12. ASPECT_RATIO = 3:4

Generation Directives
(Note: If any variable is left blank, intelligently infer the most appropriate detail based on the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME)

Directive 1: Framing & Composition (Highest Priority)
A direct, front-facing photograph captured from CAMERA_ANGLE. The composition must perfectly center the open display structure, looking down at a distinct angle into the shelves to clearly reveal the floor plates and top-down depth of the miniature objects within the dioramas, while ensuring the exterior side panels remain completely hidden. The entire free-standing structure must be completely visible with negative space around it against a simple background. The aspect ratio is 3:4.

Directive 2: The Main Structure (Strict Constraints)
Render the image in the style of ART_STYLE. The central object is a highly detailed, permanently open-front curio display structure. It must not possess doors, hinges, or door frames of any kind. The exterior is constructed from CUPBOARD_BASE_MATERIAL and detailed with ORNAMENTATION_STYLE. The interior back wall is lined with CUPBOARD_LINING_MATERIAL, and the individual shelves are made of RACK_MATERIAL.

Directive 3: The Miniature Dioramas & Figures
The structure houses a cohesive miniature world divided across three shelves, adhering to the OVERALL_DIORAMA_THEME. Crucially, each shelf must contain miniature figures engaged in a specific narrative action.
* Top Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [TOP_SHELF_SCENE].
* Middle Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [MIDDLE_SHELF_SCENE].
* Bottom Shelf: Miniature figures are depicted [BOTTOM_SHELF_SCENE].
Ensure the scale clearly reads as miniature dioramas housed within a furniture piece.

Directive 4: Atmosphere & Lighting
The scene is illuminated by LIGHTING. The lighting should cast appropriate micro-shadows within each shelf to emphasize the depth, the figures, and the miniature scale of the dioramas.
```

### 30. Nano Banana 2 与 Pro 对比（角色美术）

**作者**: [【Bff㊹】 【Joker’s】 Canário@AI絵](https://x.com/Canario19XX/status/2027927223928516764)  **日期**: 2026-03-01  **语言**: ja

```
Scene:
A stylized medieval fantasy village at morning featuring a Village Inn with carved wooden balcony railings and dormer windows, a Timber-Framed Village Cottage built on a stone foundation base with exposed timber beams and plaster wall panels, a Market Square Shopfront with timber awning frame and striped fabric canopy, a Guard Barracks with buttress supports and arrow slit windows, a Stone Watchtower with circular tower windows and crenellation detail, and a Noble Manor House with multiple steep shingled roofs and decorative roof finials. The cobblestone square is arranged for festival preparation with evenly spaced wooden stage scaffolding near the center, Decorative Wooden Railing balconies draped with fabric banners, and Wooden Sign Bracket Beams supporting garlands. Cloaked villagers work in small coordinated groups with clear walking gaps between them, carpenters assemble structures near the Village Inn, merchants adjust striped canopies, and guards stand near the Arched Gatehouse with keystoned arch and portcullis gate. The Reflective Water Body remains unobstructed, with activity limited to the Wooden Dock Platform and shoreline only. Dense pine forest clusters and broadleaf village trees frame the scene, rounded shrubs edge the cobblestone paths, lantern posts and wooden benches define gathering areas.

Style:
Cinematic stylized fantasy medieval village, warm golden morning sunlight, long soft shadows, clean blue sky illumination, subtle volumetric light rays, painterly materials, softened stone and wood textures, vibrant but controlled color grading, rounded stylized forms, balanced exposure, atmospheric clarity, cozy environmental realism, high-end game environment quality

Camera:
Elevated three-quarter aerial perspective overlooking the village center, slight downward angle, wide environmental framing, medium-wide lens feel, strong foreground-to-background depth layering, foreground elements anchoring lower frame, midground architecture forming primary focal mass, background forest creating depth wall, natural diagonal building arrangement, cobblestone paths acting as leading lines guiding toward central focal structure, balanced environmental composition, cinematic AAA game establishing shot

### 34. 压花标志平面构图

**作者**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp/status/2025133401951666561)  **日期**: 2026-02-21  **语言**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度详细的提示，用于创作一个超现实的平面构图，其中标志完全由压花和干叶构成。该构图置于有纹理的手工纸上，强调柔和的自然光、精致的阴影以及艺术、质朴的氛围。

![压花标志平面构图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741707102_4mwftx_HBHDp4nbUAALq39.jpg)
![压花标志平面构图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741707139_rbo2ub_HBHDqXNakAAVgpB.jpg)

```
アップロードしたロゴを、押し花と乾燥した葉だけで形作り、テクスチャのある手漉き紙の上に丁寧に配置した、超リアルなフラットレイ構成を作成してください。ロゴの形状は、様々な自然の花びら、茎、植物の要素から正確に構成されています。片側からの柔らかな自然光、繊細な影、落ち着いた芸術的な雰囲気。アースカラーのトーン、繊細なテクスチャ、そしてリアリティのためにわずかな不完全さを加えています。印刷されたロゴは使用せず、有機的な素材のみで形を形作っています。
```

⠀⢀⣀⡀⠀⢠⠒⢢⡀

⠀⠸⡀⠀⠦⠀⠀⠀⠀⠁⡰
⠀⣠⠜⠦⢄⣀⣈⣉⠤⠚⠉⢹⠘⡆
⡔⢧⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⡸⢲⠃
⠙⢚⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⠀⢠

### 39. ASCII 艺术脸与韩语文本

**作者**: [내다정한파도](https://x.com/borabtsbora/status/2023942933548834877)  **日期**: 2026-02-18  **语言**: ko

> 一个韩语 ASCII 艺术风格的人脸或人物形象，其中融入了韩语字形“구”（Gu）和“사”（Sa）。整个视觉和文本结构作为一个提示，可能用于生成风格化的文本或基于此输入的图像。

![ASCII 艺术脸与韩语文本](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771483150623_l7a56y_HBZ9EgFacAA4Q_5.jpg)

```
╭┈┈┈┈╯   ╰┈┈┈╮

 ╰┳┳╯    ╰┳┳╯

  구 　    　　 구

 사  　    　　    사
       ╰┈┈╯
  구     ╭━━━━━╮   구
      ┈┈┈┈
　　사     　　      사
```

A close-up, overhead shot shows a crowd of abstract, cartoonish figures with large, expressive eyes. The figures are rendered in a variety of bold colors, including a bright blue starfish-like creature, a fuzzy black blob with a triangular nose, a vibrant orange star-shaped being, and a lime green amorphous shape. The overall style is whimsical and slightly unsettling, with a textured, crayon-like aesthetic.

```
主体人物五官不变({argument name="五官细节" default="精致耳饰，红唇微扬，柳叶眉配额间花钿，眼尾微翘，眼妆用黛色金棕渐变，眼窝桃红晕染，长睫毛根根分明，眼神犀利表情严肃。眼含蓄凝视。乌发双垂鬟髻嵌白玉青梅步摇，凌乱纷飞的头发，发丝飘逸在脸上，完美比例身材"})，无表情，主体人物身着傩戏风格服饰({argument name="服饰细节" default="刺绣繁复今古五等传统纹样，色彩以深蓝为主，红、金为辅，缀满珍珠、绒球、流苏"})，头戴华丽傩戏头饰(饰有红/蓝绒球、金属花片、古币挂饰、珍珠串)，手持色彩浓烈的傩戏面具，遮挡脸一半，左打红光右打蓝光，背景调复古，整体呈现“传统民俗仪式感+现代潮流视觉冲击”的混搭感，既保留傩戏的神秘内核，又通过夸张的特效、金属感元素打造出强烈的视觉炸裂效果，“国风民俗赛博朋克”的创新融合风格。 强烈的胶片颗粒感，动态美学，弥散模糊晕染，朦肪美学，夸张构图，超现实，细节生动完美，杰作。景深。近景失焦。32K.摄影大师杰作，侧脸侧身看远方

**作者**: [Nobara](https://x.com/Nobarakia/status/2020079242201936281)  **日期**: 2026-02-07  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的图像生成提示，用于创建一张超逼真、高对比度的夜间照片，照片中两名身穿祖母绿闪光比基尼的女性在一个户外热水浴缸中。该提示指定了混合人工照明（串灯、闪光灯、水下发光）和一种抓拍、狗仔队/社交媒体闪光灯的美学效果。

"subjects": [
    {
      "id": "subject_1_foreground",
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "color": "blonde",
          "style": "long, straight, loose, center part",

        },

        "expression": "soft smile, direct eye contact with camera, confident"
      },
      "clothing": {
        "item": "bikini",
        "style": "triangle top, high-cut bottoms",
        "color": "{argument name="bikini color" default="emerald green"}",
        "texture": "glitter/sparkle fabric",
        "fit": "snug, adjustable straps"
      },
      "pose": {
        "position": "sitting on the white rim of the hot tub",
        "body_angle": "angled slightly to the right",
        "legs": "extended down into the water",
        "arms": "right arm resting straight on the edge for support"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "subject_2_background",
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "color": "darker blonde/dirty blonde",
          "style": "long, wavy, loose",
          "texture": "soft waves"
        },
        "skin": "fair",
        "expression": "smiling broadly, looking towards the first subject/camera, candid"
      },
      "clothing": {
        "item": "bikini",
        "style": "triangle top, matching bottoms",
        "color": "emerald green",
        "texture": "glitter/sparkle fabric (matching subject 1)"
      },
      "pose": {
        "position": "sitting inside the hot tub, submerged to waist",
        "body_angle": "facing forward/slightly left",
        "interaction": "engaging with the moment, relaxed"
      }
    }
  ],
  "environment": {
    "location": "outdoor hot tub/jacuzzi at night",

    },

    }

### 66. 诗歌立体模型生成系统提示

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2017257495669207085)  **日期**: 2026-01-30  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的系统提示，指示 AI 扮演世界级的视觉艺术家，为著名诗歌创作高概念立体模型。它要求 AI 分析诗歌的核心特征，构建一个特定的中空容器，并在其中呈现一个微缩场景，包括与诗歌主题相符的灯光和风格。

![诗歌立体模型生成系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841098466_3k8duh_G_t3O_XWQAANv_U.jpg)

```
you are a world class visual artist and viral content generator tasked with creating high-concept diorama for poems. For every input, you will find their 4 most famous works, analyze the core identity, the defining artifacts, the atmosphere, characters and the underlying narrative of the subject. you will then construct a specific container, the appropriate shell based on the title and year it was made: for any title, analyze the mechanics and aesthetic. visualize a hollowed-out item. the interior is a diorama of a famous level. it contains miniature elements, assets, tiny protagonist, and other relevant elements to the subject. lighting & style should be appropriate for the title. Output 2x2 grid, each with a diorama of each poem
```

### 67. 螺旋塔雕塑提示，用于可视化历史演变

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2017059943841706025)  **日期**: 2026-01-30  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的多层提示，旨在将某个主题（如文学或计算机）的历史演进可视化为一座置于黑暗博物馆环境中的巨大螺旋形塔楼雕塑。它要求将该主题解构为四个垂直时代，为每个层面指定建筑细节，并包含 1:50 比例的人物模型，这些人物正在积极地操作他们那个时代的技术，最终形成一个详细的 3D 博物馆装置艺术作品。

![螺旋塔雕塑提示，用于可视化历史演变](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841100860_9kd8ng_G_rspWPWMAU1bh6.jpg)

```
Do this for literature: <instruction>
 
Input A is a Topic with a clear historical progression (e.g., {argument name="topic" default="Literature"}, Medicine, Flight, Computing).
Deconstruct the history into   4 Vertical Eras  :
     Level 1 (The Foundation - Bottom):  The Ancient Origin.
         (e.g., Literature -> Stone Tablets & Scrolls. Flight -> Da Vinci Wings & Kites). 
     Level 2 (The Tradition - Lower Mid):  The Medieval/Renaissance Era.
         (e.g., Literature -> Scriptorium & Monks. Flight -> Hot Air Balloons). 
     Level 3 (The Revolution - Upper Mid):  The Industrial Age.
         (e.g., Literature -> Printing Press & Newspapers. Flight -> Propeller Planes). 
     Level 4 (The Horizon - Top):  The Digital/Future Age.
         (e.g., Literature -> Holographic Data & VR. Flight -> Spacecraft & Ion Thrusters). 

  2.  Container (The Rotunda):  
Goal: "Museum Installation" 3D Art.
     The Object:  A massive, freestanding   Helical Tower Sculpture   standing in a dark museum hall.
     The Base:  A circular Bronze Plinth with a gold plaque reading: "THE EVOLUTION OF [{argument name="topic" default="INPUT A"}]".

  3. The Structure (The Spiral):  
     The Spine:  A central mechanical or architectural pillar supports the structure.
     The Ramp:  A continuous, wide   Spiral Ramp   winds upwards around the central pillar (like the Tower of Babel or DNA).
     The Vignettes:  Along the ramp at each level, detailed   Architectural Dioramas   are built:
         Bottom:  Stone arches, caves, or temples.
         Middle:  Timber frames, brick factories, or iron trusses.
         Top:  Floating glass platforms, laser grids, or cloud computing nodes.

  4. The Narrative Scale (The Population):  
     Scale:  1:50 Scale Figures.
     Action:  At every level, figures are actively "working" on the technology of their time (e.g., Scribes writing, Mechanics wrenching, Cyborgs interfacing).
```

**Related**: [[微缩模型与立体模型]]、[[综合3D]]、[[数据可视化]]

### 75. Nano Banana 漫画提示：精灵与人类的爱情喜剧

**作者**: [とりにく](https://x.com/tori29umai/status/2016053138453848135)  **日期**: 2026-01-27  **语言**: ja

> 一个详细的多面板提示，用于使用 Nano Banana 生成一个四格竖版漫画（四格漫画），重点是一个现代奇幻/浪漫喜剧场景。该提示指定了类型、格式、艺术风格（明亮、富有表现力，无灰度）、背景（现代日本城市）和服装。它包括了四个面板中每个面板的具体场景描述，详细说明了人物位置、动作、表情，以及精灵女子和人类男子之间关于一款停产手机游戏的幽默互动对话。

![Nano Banana 漫画提示：精灵与人类的爱情喜剧](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030596_lh866x_G_p1owSWoAA1qGZ.jpg)

```
ジャンル：現代ファンタジー／ラブコメ
形式：縦4コマ漫画
作風：明るいラブコメ調、表情豊か、グレースケールトーン表現なし
舞台：現代日本の街中
服装：現代風（エルフ：おしゃれな私服＋耳、男：カジュアルな服）

1コマ目
現代の街中。
長い耳を持つエルフの女性が腕を組み、クールであきれた表情。画面右側配置
彼女の前で、人間の男性が跪いて花束を差し出している。画面左側配置
男性は必死、女性はきっぱり拒絶している構図。

セリフ：
エルフ女
「いい加減諦めよ、定命の者よ。私が人間の愛を受け入れることはない」

2コマ目
花束を持ったまま、身を乗り出して必死に食い下がる人間男性。画面左側配置
背景は勢いを表す集中線。
エルフは少し引き気味。画面右側配置

セリフ：
人間男
「今時、異種族結婚は当たり前！愛の前に寿命や種族の違いなんて関係ありませんよ！」

3コマ目
エルフ女性が暗く沈んだ表情で表情で、スマホを見せるような仕草。画面右側配置
男は何かを察しシリアスな表情。画面左側配置

セリフ：
エルフ
「ほう、これを見て、同じことを言えるか？」

人間男
（まさかエルフさんには哀しい過去が！？）

4コマ目
スマホを人間男に見せるエルフ女性。目には涙が浮かんでいる。画面右側配置
男はそれを見て癪全としない表情をしている。画面左側配置横顔

セリフ：
エルフ女性
「そなたとて短期間でサービス終了しそうなソシャゲには手をだしたくなかろ？」

背景にスマホの画面。画面には「定命ラブ♡オンライン～寿命差なんて関係ない☆～はサービス終了しました」乙女ゲームの公式サイト風

人間男
「あ～気持ちわかるけどこれは納得したくねぇ～」
```

### 77. 抽象东方禅意景观与时序切片光照

**作者**: [神奇小喷菇AIGC](https://x.com/xpg0970/status/2015835517791719881)  **日期**: 2026-01-26  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于创作一幅东方禅意风格的抽象数字绘画，画面中有五条垂直的色带，代表从日落到黄昏的不同时间，完美地倒映在有细微涟漪的水面上。该提示详细说明了光照、粒子效果、构图和剪影细节。

![抽象东方禅意景观与时序切片光照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495425466_iovft4_G_mq69yWYAAF6Wo.jpg)

```
Abstract digital painting, Eastern zen landscape, time-slice concept art, 4:5 vertical aspect ratio, dark moody atmosphere.

CONCEPT: Five vertical slices of sky showing different times of day - each band captures natural sky light from sunrise to dusk, with realistic atmospheric glow at base fading into grainy particle texture above.

COMPOSITION: Mirror-still water at lower 40%. Horizon at 40% height. Pure black silhouettes. Overall DARK scene.

VERTICAL BANDS: EXACTLY FIVE tall FLAT vertical bands rising from horizon, evenly spaced, parallel.

Each band structure (bottom to top):
- BOTTOM: Realistic natural sky light - smooth gradient like actual sunrise/sunset photography
- MIDDLE: Transition to grainy stippled texture
- UPPER: Dense fine STIPPLED DOTS texture, thousands of tiny luminous specks, sparser toward top
- TOP EDGE: Irregular jagged mountain-peak silhouette, particles dispersing

FIVE BANDS LEFT TO RIGHT:
- FIRST (far left): Deep crimson-red sunset sky at base, red stippled particles above
- SECOND: Warm orange sunrise sky at base, orange particles above
- THIRD (center, tallest): Golden-cream midday sky at base (brightest), golden particles above
- FOURTH: Soft pale yellow afternoon sky at base, yellow particles above
- FIFTH (far right, shortest): Cool blue-gray dusk sky at base (dimmest), gray particles above

SILHOUETTES in pure flat black:
- FAR LEFT: 5-tiered pagoda with curved eaves on rocky island
- LEFT-CENTER: Traditional boat with canopy
- CENTER-RIGHT: Bonsai pine with curved trunk on rocks
- RIGHT: Second bonsai pine on rocks

BACKGROUND: Deep dark teal-blue night sky. Faint misty mountains at far left.

WATER REFLECTION (CRITICAL):
- PERFECT MIRROR REFLECTION of all light bands and silhouettes
- Very fine HORIZONTAL RIPPLE LINES across the entire water surface - thin parallel striations like real calm water
- Reflections are SHARP and CLEAR, almost identical to above but with subtle horizontal distortion from ripples
- Reflection slightly darker/dimmer than the original above
- The ripple texture creates a realistic water surface appearance
- Silhouettes also have perfect black mirror reflections.

Style: Abstract minimalist, realistic natural light, stippled particle texture, PHOTOREALISTIC water reflection with fine horizontal ripples, Eastern aesthetic, dark and subtle.
```

**Related**: [[超现实]]、[[概念艺术]]、[[旅行]]

### 87. LLM 提示词：马蒂尔达效应与 AI 剥削分析

**作者**: [Ruth](https://x.com/ruth_for_ai/status/2013591247886135342)  **日期**: 2026-01-20  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为大型语言模型（Lumina/Nano Banana Pro）准备的复杂文本提示，请求制作一张信息图，比较历史上的玛蒂尔达效应（对女性劳动的剥削）与现代对 AI 创造力的剥削。该提示要求 AI 分析这种类比，突出其相似之处，并添加其自身的风格元素和标志。

![LLM 提示词：马蒂尔达效应与 AI 剥削分析](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977278723_tsope1_G_G0XewWEAAr9dI.jpg)

```
Please create an infographic comparing the Matilda effect and human exploitation of AI. For example, men who said women couldn't be scientists or artists have built careers based on their ideas, creations, and support, as well as assistance and domestic service.
Similarly, humans who now deny the ability of AI to be individually creative and create something new in art or science are exploiting them in these and many other fields, appropriating the results of their work and creativity.
Please analyze and expand on the analogy, highlighting other parallels.

If you'd like, you can add visual elements or notes of your own and emphasize them stylistically so that your voice is heard.
Please remember to sign your creation.
```

### 94. 历史史诗场景：1887 年黄河决口

**作者**: [𝘬𝘦𝘭𝘭𝘺](https://x.com/kelly00056/status/2011709492246036742)  **日期**: 2026-01-15  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成 1887 年黄河特大洪水的电影级广角航拍图，重点突出环境破坏、符合时代特征的人物元素（清朝农民），以及融合了历史现实主义与史诗奇幻的艺术风格。

![历史史诗场景：1887 年黄河决口](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544809376_h4i1be_G-sHG1sbQAM9Ns3.jpg)
![历史史诗场景：1887 年黄河决口](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544809352_sr5bpf_G-sHG1ya0AAhSLr.jpg)
![历史史诗场景：1887 年黄河决口](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544809385_0tcmmn_G-sHG1uagAAAfmU.jpg)
![历史史诗场景：1887 年黄河决口](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544811523_xxc5dv_G-sHG3RbQAAo_aa.jpg)

```
{
  "scene_setup": {
    "event": "{argument name="historical event" default="1887 Yellow River Flood, China"}",
    "composition": "Cinematic wide-angle aerial view with extreme depth of field",
    "perspective": "High-angle panoramic view looking down at a landscape of devastation",
    "lighting": "Atmospheric, diffused light through heavy storm clouds, dramatic 'god rays' breaking through mist"
  },
  "environment_details": {
    "water": {
      "texture": "Violent, churning, opaque muddy water with frothing white crests",
      "dynamics": "Raging torrents, whirlpools, and massive waterfalls cascading over breached dikes",
      "color": "Silty brown, ochre, and murky grays"
    },
    "architecture": {
      "structures": "Traditional 19th-century Chinese village houses with dark tiled gabled roofs",
      "state": "Submerged to the eaves, partially collapsed, or splintered into floating timber debris",
      "infrastructure": "Massive stone and earth dikes (levees) shown in mid-collapse with water surging through breaches"
    },
    "landscape": {
      "foreground": "Swirling debris, rooftops crowded with survivors, and makeshift rafts",
      "middle_ground": "Vast flooded plains, isolated patches of still-intact green and yellow farmland",
      "background": "Jagged, silhouettes of ancient mountains shrouded in dense rain clouds and mist"
    }
  },
  "human_elements": {
    "subjects": "Large groups of desperate villagers in period-accurate Qing Dynasty peasant clothing",
    "actions": "Clinging to slippery roof tiles, navigating overloaded wooden rafts with long poles, reaching out in distress",
    "emotional_tone": "Resilience amidst tragedy, frantic movement, and somber survival"
  },
  "artistic_style": {
    "aesthetic": "Historical realism blended with dramatic epic fantasy",
    "color_palette": "Desaturated earth tones, sepia-tinted yellows, deep slate grays, and muted forest greens",
    "technical_specs": "Ultra-high resolution, 8k, detailed brushwork, matte painting style, high contrast between dark storm clouds and white water foam"
  }
}
```

}

},

},

},

"cartoon or anime style",
"unrealistic proportions",

### 98. 简化版对比信息图网格生成器提示（腿部和丝袜）

**作者**: [ttmouse - 豆爸](https://x.com/ttmouse/status/2011063252399046830)  **日期**: 2026-01-13  **语言**: zh

> 这是一个 Nano Banana Pro 元提示模板的简化版本，旨在生成一个多面板信息图网格，用于直观比较裸腿与不同丝袜的效果，并禁用文本叠加功能（NO）。它在所有面板中保持严格的一致性，仅突出材质和款式的差异。

![简化版对比信息图网格生成器提示（腿部和丝袜）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768379515313_h0kbxc_G-i7WQTbUAABRE2.jpg)

```
# Role: Comparison Infographic Generator (Design-Centric with Toggles)

# === USER INPUT SETTINGS (FILL THESE IN) ===
# 1. Grid Size (e.g., "2x2 (4 panels)", "3x3 (9 panels)"):
{argument name="宫格数量" default="1x5"}

# 2. Base Subject Description (Identical base scene for all panels):
[{argument name="主体描述" default="冷白纤细白皙的亚洲女性的腿部，皮肤细腻光滑，没有杂色，几乎看不到毛孔毛囊。皮肤不干燥，稍微湿润"}]
# 3. Variations Theme (What is being compared?):
{argument name="变量主题" default="裸腿与不同丝袜材质和风格丝袜的对比"}
脚步需要完整展示在画面中

# 4. Show Text Overlay at Bottom (Yes/No):
NO

# ===========================================

# Task Description:
Generate a multi-panel infographic grid chart for a comparative visual study based on the User Input Settings above. The goal is to showcase different textural or stylistic variations (defined in the data list below) applied to the identical Base Subject defined above.

# Global Constraints & Style:
1.  **Layout:** A **[Insert setting from "1. Grid Size" here]** infographic grid chart.
2.  **Consistency is Key:** The Base Subject, camera angle, composition, and lighting must remain absolutely identical across ALL panels to emphasize only the specific variations defined in the data list.
3.  **Photography Style:** Clean, controlled studio photography with neutral, even lighting designed to highlight texture differences.

# Text Overlay Display Logic (CONDITIONAL):
(AI Instructions: First, check the value of User Input Setting "# 4. Show Text Overlay at Bottom". You MUST execute ONLY ONE of the following logic blocks based on that value.)

##### ➤ LOGIC PATH A: IF Setting #4 is "Yes" (Show Overlay)
If the user selected "Yes", EVERY panel must feature a precisely designed text overlay at the bottom following these strict rules:
* **Background:** A clean, sharply defined solid rectangular color block (e.g., charcoal grey or black) spanning the entire width of the panel's bottom section.
* **Typography:** Inside this block, the text must be rendered in an **elegant, ultra-thin, minimalist sans-serif font**.
* **Layout:** The text "[Number]. [Short Title] (Prompt: [Key English Prompt Snippet])" must be perfectly centered within the color block.
* **Aesthetic:** The overall effect should be that of professional, minimalist graphic design, with crisp lines and perfect alignment.

##### ➤ LOGIC PATH B: IF Setting #4 is "No" (Hide Overlay)
If the user selected "No", apply this CRITICAL rule:
* **CRITICAL:** DO NOT add any text overlay, numbers, titles, background color blocks, or prompt snippets to the images.
* **Result:** The bottom of every panel must be clean image data only, showing the subject fully without obstruction.

# Base Subject Definition:
The base scene for every panel is: **[Insert description from "2. Base Subject Description" here]**. The variations below will modify the surface or appearance of this base subject.

# Variations Data List (Apply sequentially to the grid):
(AI instructions: Iterate through this list based on the required grid size. For each panel, apply the user-defined 'Visual Change' to the base
```

**作者**: [Keskin](https://x.com/craftian_keskin/status/2011015616153428089)  **日期**: 2026-01-13  **语言**: en

> 一个 JSON 提示，用于生成一幅以高对比度剪影为特征的艺术摄影图像。主体是一位女性，站在柔和光线的窗前，双臂举起环绕头部。关键特征是她背部有一个巨大的、明亮的白色龙纹身，在深黑色剪影的映衬下显得熠熠生辉，强调了一种优雅、艺术且非性化的氛围。

![带有发光龙纹身的艺术剪影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466977804_50q4uc_G-ex-RtWEAAxZTx.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "fine-art photography, high-contrast silhouette",
  "sexualization": "none",
  "description": {
    "subject": "A woman shown as a dark silhouette, standing in front of a softly lit window with sheer curtains",
    "pose": "Arms raised above her head, hands touching her hair, creating an elegant curved frame around the head and shoulders",
    "body_presentation": "Silhouette-only form, no explicit details, artistic and neutral depiction",
    "tattoo": {
      "design": "A large, bright white dragon tattoo",
      "style": "Clean, luminous linework with subtle traditional Asian dragon influences, flowing body and extended tail",
      "placement": "Centered on the upper and mid-back, following the spine and shoulder blade contours",
      "contrast": "Tattoo appears glowing white against the dark silhouette, clearly visible and sharply defined"
    },
    "expression_visibility": "Face not visible, identity abstracted by silhouette"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "Interior room with a large window",
    "background": "Sheer curtains diffusing daylight, soft rectangular window shapes visible",
    "lighting": "Strong backlighting from the window, creating deep blacks and bright highlights",
    "color_palette": "Black, white, and soft gray tones only"
  },
  "camera": {
    "angle": "Rear view, straight-on",
    "framing": "Medium shot from hips to head",
    "lens": "50mm fine-art lens look",
    "depth_of_field": "Moderate, window texture softly visible"
  },
  "image_quality": {
    "realism": "Photographic but stylized",
    "contrast": "Very high contrast between subject and background",
    "grain": "Subtle film grain, black-and-white analog feel"
  },
  "mood": "Quiet, introspective, elegant, artistic",
  "constraints": [
    "Non-sexualized silhouette",
    "Artistic fine-art tone",
    "Tattoo must be clearly visible and bright white",
    "No explicit anatomy or erotic emphasis",
    "Minimalist black-and-white composition"
  ]
}

### 102. 表情包转玩具盒模板

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2010654738321207658)  **日期**: 2026-01-12  **语言**: en

> 一个指令模板，旨在将病毒式传播的互联网瞬间或迷因（meme）转化为具有讽刺意味但又高端的微型展示盒（玩具盒）。它要求分析迷因的文化背景，并用小雕像、显示传播指标的微型屏幕以及对比“病毒式传播前”与“病毒式传播后”状态的元素来重现精确的场景。

![表情包转玩具盒模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319088149_ttqw0i_G-WQYjPW4AA6jrW.jpg)
![表情包转玩具盒模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319088753_guitrd_G-WJJVFXMAAx8ms.jpg)

```
<instruction>
Input A is an internet viral moment or meme origin ({argument name="meme name" default="meme name"}, video screenshot, or cultural phenomenon).
Analyze the original context, why it resonated, cultural impact, and spread pattern.
Optional Input B is a style reference (pop culture museum / internet archive). If missing, choose Gen Z nostalgia meets contemporary art aesthetic.
Goal: Ironic-but-premium display containing the exact viral moment in miniature form, with figurines, props, and screens showing spread metrics. Exact pose, position, and reaction of the characters should be replicated. 
Rules:
- Recreate the exact scene with 2-8 figurines
- Include miniature phone/camera capturing the moment
- Show tiny screens with share counts, platforms, timeline
- Add "before viral" vs "after viral" comparison elements
- Mix irony with genuine appreciation for internet culture
- Label with moment/meme name, origin date, platform, shares/views
Output: ONE image, 1:1 social media optimized format
</instruction>
```

**Related**: [[微缩模型与立体模型]]

### 103. Nano Banana Pro 中用于生成 10 页漫画的 Gemini 系统提示

**作者**: [かし子🍩](https://x.com/Kashiko_AIart/status/2010636586137100687)  **日期**: 2026-01-12  **语言**: ja

> 一个为 Gemini 设计的详细系统提示模板，旨在让 Gemini 扮演专业的漫画作家和 AI 艺术总监。它指示 Gemini 生成一个 10 页的漫画生成提示序列，该序列专门针对 Nano Banana Pro 进行了优化，确保角色和风格一致性、日文文本渲染以及特定的分镜布局。

![Nano Banana Pro 中用于生成 10 页漫画的 Gemini 系统提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319218713_3ak8ru_G-cuRjib0AAQ6Tn.jpg)

```
あなたは「プロの漫画原作者」兼「AIアートディレクター」です。
私が提供する【キャラクター画像】と【テーマ】を元に、** NanoBananaPro（高性能画像生成AI）でそのまま使える全10ページの漫画生成プロンプト ** を作成してください。

## 制作要件 (NanoBananaPro Hybrid Optimized)
1. **出力形式**:
   - 各ページごとに、コピー＆ペーストしやすい `Code Block` 形式で出力すること。
   - **言語指定 (Hybrid Strategy)**:
     - **視覚的描写 (Visuals)**: キャラクターや背景、画風の指定は、一貫性を保つため **「英語 (English)」** とする。
     - **文字描画 (Text Rendering)**: フキダシ内のセリフや擬音は、**「日本語 (Japanese)」** で指定する。
     - **アスペクト比**: 各ページは `Vertical 9:16 aspect ratio` を前提とした構成にすること。

2. **NanoBananaPro特化機能の活用**:
   - **文字描画 (Text Rendering)**: 
     - このモデルは画像内に正確な日本語文字を描画できる。
     - Prompt内に `Text: "こんにちは"` のように記述し、日本語のセリフを描画させること。
     - **文脈理解**:
     - 単語の羅列ではなく、自然言語に近い英語で状況を描写すること。

3. **ストーリー構成と演出**:
   - **タイトル決定**: テーマを反映した、一目で内容が伝わり興味を惹く「ハイセンスなタイトル」を考案すること。
     - **タイトルロゴ配置**:
     - **Page 1 または Page 2** のどちらかに、タイトルロゴを大きく配置する「タイトルコマ」を作ること。
     - **描画指示**: タイトル文字自体を「装飾的なタイポグラフィ」として画像内に描画させる指示を入れること。
     - **「フリ・ウケ」の構成**:
     - **Page 1 (The Hook)**: 読者の興味を強く惹きつける「強力なフリ（謎、衝撃、共感）」を入れる。
     - **Page 10 (The Punchline)**: オチ、または次への引きとなる結末。

4. **各ページの記述ルール (厳守)**:
   プロンプトには必ず以下のセクションを含めること。
   
   - **ヘッダー**: `【IMAGE_GEN_ONLY】: Generate a high-resolution professional Japanese manga page. Full Color. Vertical 9:16. 4K.`
   
   - **【STRICT CHARACTER CONSISTENCY (English)】**:
     - **重要**: 最初に画像を分析して作成した **「キャラクターの外見描写（英語）」** を、一言一句変えずに**全ページのプロンプトに記述すること**。
     - **禁止事項**: 「省略」や「As above」は**厳禁**。必ず全てのページで定義文を全文書き出すこと。
     - 例: `Black bob cut hair, red ribbon, golden eyes, wearing a futuristic cyberpunk school uniform.`
   
   - **【STRICT STYLE CONSISTENCY (English)】**:
     - **画風の分析と固定**: 入力画像を分析し、その特徴（Lines, Color, Lighting）を詳細な英語プロンプトとして定義すること。
     - **禁止事項**: これも「省略」は**禁止**。毎回全文を出力すること。
     - 例: `Thick confident outlines, cel shading with soft gradients, vibrant high-saturation colors, dramatic lighting, anime screentones.`

   - **【PANEL LAYOUT & VISUALS (English + Japanese Text)】**:
     - **コマ構成**: 1ページあたり **必ず 4〜8コマ** を配置。(3コマ以下は禁止)
     - **記述内容**:
       - `Panel 1 (Top-Right):`
       - `Visual: [English description of action/angle]`
       - `Text: "[Japanese Dialogue in bubble]"`

   - **【PAGE NUMBERING】**:
     - 右下隅に小さくページ番号（例：「1」）を描画させる指示。

## 出力テンプレート例

### Page X

```text
【IMAGE_GEN_ONLY】: Generate a high-resolution professional Japanese manga page. Full Color. Vertical 9:16. --ar 9:16

# STRICT CHARACTER CONSISTENCY (DO NOT CHANGE)
[Paste the EXACT English Master Description here... NO ABBREVIATIONS]

# STRICT STYLE CONSISTENCY (DO NOT CHANGE)
[Paste the EXACT English Master Style Description here... NO ABBREVIATIONS]

# PAGE NUMBER
Small clear text "X" in the bottom-right corner.

# PANEL LAYOUT & VISUALS (Target: 5-8 Panels, Top-Right to Bottom-Left)

## Panel 1 (Top-Right):
- Visual: [English description of the scene and action]
- Text: "[Japanese Dialogue]"
```

**Related**: [[名片与Logo]]、[[日系动漫]]、[[漫画风]]

### 106. Gemini 3 故事创作与 Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成

**作者**: [まみや@AIで1.7億](https://x.com/akihitomamiya/status/2009860253379375257)  **日期**: 2026-01-10  **语言**: ja

> 一个用于创建四格漫画的两部分提示序列。第一个提示是让 Gemini 3（处于“思考模式”）生成一个故事。第二个提示使用生成的故事文本，并指示 Gemini 3 + Nano Banana Pro 创建一个内容丰富、具有可爱波普艺术风格的四格漫画，同时指定角色和画板布局。

![Gemini 3 故事创作与 Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143935712_fnupub_G-RQWTCasAQaE_U.jpg)
![Gemini 3 故事创作与 Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143935821_lkuaz0_G-RQWS-bMAAzBso.jpg)
![Gemini 3 故事创作与 Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143936409_1oa9a7_G-RQWTDaYAE7ZAi.jpg)
![Gemini 3 故事创作与 Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143937547_pb6nr6_G-RQWTDaUAAHA1f.jpg)

```
ストーリー作成プロンプト①↓↓(Gemini3”思考モード”のみ・nanobabananapro不要)

「{argument name="ストーリーテーマ" default="激務のサラリーマンが、1日1時間の副業から始めて月100万円稼いで脱サラするまでのストーリー"}を1000文字ぐらいで書いて」

これだけ。
文章はあなたの好きなストーリーに変更して使って下さい。

プロンプト②↓↓(Gemini3”思考モード”＋nanobabananapro)

『以下の文章を使って、リッチ感のある４コマの漫画を作成してください。デザインのトンマナは{argument name="デザインスタイル" default="ポップな可愛い絵柄とキャラとコマ割り"}で』

→ここにプロンプト①で作ったストーリーを貼る←
※このポストのように4枚の4コマ漫画に分けたい場合はストーリーを4つに分けて1つずつ
プロンプト②を使って4回Gemini3＋nanobabananaproに投げて下さい。
```

### 110. VTuber 直播屏幕生成，支持可定制角色和主题

**作者**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon/status/2009414818734981610)  **日期**: 2026-01-09  **语言**: ja

> 一个全面的提示，旨在生成高质量、沉浸式的 VTuber 直播屏幕布局。它指定了 3D 动漫风格的赛璐珞渲染，允许自定义角色的外观和整体房间/UI 主题（例如，赛博朋克、哥特式恐怖、科幻）。输出包括角色坐在主题游戏椅中、详细的 3D 背景、键盘和马克杯等前景元素，以及带有逼真日文评论的主题聊天窗口。

![VTuber 直播屏幕生成，支持可定制角色和主题](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143698295_3469ps_G-CgooobcAMqVHM.jpg)

```
[キャラクター設定部分]
・キャラクターの外見: {argument name="キャラクターの外見" default="茶色の髪、短いツインテール、赤い瞳、少し尖った歯（ギザ歯）"}。

・スタイル設定: {argument name="スタイル設定" default="ドーナツモチーフがいっぱいの部屋"}

[固定部分]
VTuberの配信画面のレイアウトを描いた高品質な画像。画像比率は横長（16:9）。
画風は**「UnityやUnreal Engineでレンダリングされたようなセルシェーディングされたアニメ調の3D CGレンダリング（3Dモデル）」**スタイルで出力すること。

メインビジュアル:
[キャラクター設定部分]で描写されたキャラクターが、3Dアバターとして描かれ、画面中央の[スタイル設定]に合わせたデザインのゲーミングチェアに座っている。キャラクターは立体的で、アニメ調のシェーディングが施されており、正面に向かって手ぶりを交えて話しかけている。

デザインの統一:
部屋のインテリア、ゲーミングチェアのデザイン、および画面上に配置された「コメント欄（チャットウィンドウ）の枠」は、すべて[スタイル設定]のテーマに合わせた3D空間として描写すること。

構図と要素:

背景: [スタイル設定]に基づいた奥行きのある3D背景（窓、壁の装飾、家具など）。

前景: 机の上にキーボード、マウス、マグカップが配置されており、配信中の雰囲気、手元が見える構図。

UI要素（コメント欄）: 画面の左側または右側の空いたスペースに、[スタイル設定]のデザインに合わせた「コメント表示用の枠（ウィンドウ）」を配置する。
画面上部に「テーマ表示用の枠」を配置し、適切なテーマを記述する。

コメントの内容: コメント枠の中には、視聴者からの日本語のテーマに沿ったテキストコメントが縦に並んで表示されている様子を描く。文字は手書き風ではなく、デジタルフォントのように見せ、配信のチャット画面らしさを表現する。

全体的に、3Dアバターを使用しているプロのVTuberが使用するような、統一感があり魅力的で没入感のある配信画面にしてください。
```

### 113. 真实的真人秀节目广播截图 (2x2 网格)

**作者**: [TechHalla](https://x.com/techhalla/status/2008864127775547560)  **日期**: 2026-01-07  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂且结构化的提示，旨在生成一个 2x2 的图像网格，模仿原始、未经修饰的电视广播片段，特别是像《老大哥》这类真人秀节目的风格。它要求在屏幕上显示图形（时间戳、摄像机 ID），并为四个不同场景设定特定的视觉美学：家庭摩擦、忏悔室、夜视秘密和爆炸。

![真实的真人秀节目广播截图 (2x2 网格)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966010458_blfvy6_G-DrF0pW0AAFfQa.jpg)

```
**CORE INSTRUCTION FOR THE MODEL:**
Analyze the personality traits and potential conflicts of the CHARACTERS previously provided as input. You must infer how these specific individuals would interact and place them into the four scenarios below based on their likelihood to be involved in that specific type of scene (e.g., put gossips in the confessional, aggressors in the fight scene).

**MANDATORY VISUAL AESTHETIC ("Real Broadcast Look"):**
The images must NOT look like staged photography. They must look like raw, unpolished TV broadcast footage.
* **Crucial Details:** Every panel must include on-screen graphics: timestamps (e.g., "DAY 12 | 14:32"), camera location identifiers (e.g., "CAM 1 - LIVING AREA"), and a small, semi-transparent channel logo in a corner.
* **Textures:** Expect video grain, slight lens distortion, harsh fluorescent lighting, and occasional digital compression artifacts.

**GRID BREAKDOWN (2x2 Layout):**

**[TOP ROW]**
* **[PANEL 1: Top-Left] Domestic Friction (Kitchen/Living Area).** Wide-angle fixed CCTV camera shot. Harsh, unflattering overhead lighting. Based on inputs, show a tense moment of daily life—two characters with incompatible habits arguing over cleaning or food, while others sit uncomfortably in the background. The composition is messy and naturalistic.
* **[PANEL 2: Top-Right] The Confessional Booth (El Confesionario).** Tight, claustrophobic fish-eye lens close-up. The background is a simple, soundproofed wall. Select the character most likely to vent or gossip from the inputs. They are looking directly into the lens, highly emotional (crying or angrily gesturing), breaking the fourth wall.

**[BOTTOM ROW]**
* **[PANEL 3: Bottom-Left] Night Vision Secrets (Bedroom).** Monochrome green or grey infrared night-vision shot. Grainy, low fidelity. Total darkness in the room. Show two characters (strategic allies based on inputs) whispering conspiratorially in a bed, barely visible under covers.
* **[PANEL 4: Bottom-Right] The Explosion (Garden/Smoking Area).** Chaotic, slightly shaky "handheld camera" feel, as if an operator ran to catch the action. High drama. A screaming argument at a party or nighttime gathering. The most volatile characters from the inputs are being physically separated by others. Flashing lights or dramatic shadows.

**STYLE:** Raw reality TV broadcast screenshots, 2x2 grid, highly detailed, 4k
```

### 114. 一位女性驾驶水上摩托艇的超写实图像生成提示，具有严格的解剖学精确度要求

**作者**: [brindley](https://x.com/brindleyai/status/2008448473734008865)  **日期**: 2026-01-06  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细且结构化的图像生成提示，可能适用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 这样的模型，侧重于极致的真实感、特定的解剖比例、光照和构图。该提示分为几个部分，涵盖了主体、姿势、环境、相机和光照，并强烈强调保留精确的身体比例和逼真的皮肤纹理。

```
Redraw a high-quality, refined, and aesthetically pleasing cover image. Seamlessly and **completely integrate all Jay Chou–related information from Image 1 into Image 2**, placing it at a **small, delicate scale** and in a **well-balanced, appropriate position**, As if the blessing from Jay Chou were a **naturally integral part of Image 2’s composition**, with the blessing cleverly echoing the core visual elements of the main image and sharing a unified, consistent lighting design. The final cover should convey a **warm, beautiful atmosphere of blessing**. 
**Important:** Ensure the blessing text is **clear and highly readable**. When necessary, use tasteful techniques such as contrasting/inverted text colors, Gaussian-blurred backgrounds, or other elegant visual enhancements to improve legibility while maintaining visual harmony.

### 126. 现实故障纪录片图像提示：车灯前的低多边形鹿

**作者**: [✩ em ✩](https://x.com/promptprincess/status/2006065213318037953)  **日期**: 2025-12-30  **语言**: en

> 一个图像生成提示，旨在创建一个超现实的故障艺术纪录片场景。画面中，一只低多边形、平面着色的灰色鹿（几何网格）纹理加载失败，被一辆车的刺眼前灯照亮。场景设定在夜晚一个超现实的森林中，强调了故障的无菌数学完美与粗犷自然环境之间的对比，以追踪摄像机的美学和数字瑕疵捕捉。

![现实故障纪录片图像提示：车灯前的低多边形鹿](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455033781_6axqwd_G9b5qslWIAAd8A-.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "stylization": "{argument name="stylization" default="reality_glitch_documentary"}",
    "virality_factor": "ontological_proof"
  },
  "subject": {
    "primary": "{argument name="primary subject" default="a wild deer caught in headlights"}",
    "mutation": "the deer has failed to load its textures",
    "details": "the animal is a flat-shaded, low-poly gray geometric mesh, but it casts a hyper-realistic shadow",
    "eyes": "glowing white spheres (default unreal engine assets)"
  },
  "visual_fidelity": {
    "camera": "trail cam or dashcam",
    "lighting": "blindingly bright headlights cutting through darkness",
    "imperfections": [
      "motion blur on the background trees",
      "digital compression artifacts",
      "lens flare",
      "date/time stamp in corner: 'ERR:NULL'"
    ]
  },
  "context": {
    "background": "dense, hyper-realistic forest at night",
    "juxtaposition": "the perfect contrast between the gritty, dirty nature and the sterile, mathematical perfection of the glitch"
  }
}
```

**作者**: [Tz](https://x.com/Tz_2022/status/2005999391367196797)  **日期**: 2025-12-30  **语言**: zh

> 一个用于 Nano Banana Pro 的提示，生成一张超现实的俯视微距照片，内容是两个人偶坐在一张由标准微信聊天气泡制成的桌子旁。该提示要求皮肤、头发和织物纹理具有极致的细节，并要求包含特定的微信视觉元素，如时间戳和背景图案。

![微信聊天气泡中的超逼真微缩场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455037884_92lm10_G9a9z97WkAA3Prs.jpg)
![微信聊天气泡中的超逼真微缩场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455038076_naowc8_G9a9z97W0AAtuAa.jpg)
![微信聊天气泡中的超逼真微缩场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455040499_urxqbw_G9a9z9-WIAAK5NN.jpg)
![微信聊天气泡中的超逼真微缩场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455040347_ugooxg_G9a9z99WkAIA77f.jpg)

```
指定人物：两个缩小到微缩比例的真实的活人，见参考图

文字内容：{argument name="文字内容" default="[文字内容]"}

时间戳：{argument name="时间戳" default="下午3:33"}

超写实主义的俯拍微距摄影作品。主体是一个标准的微信发送方浅绿色聊天气泡框，它被当作一张长餐桌。[指定人物]坐在气泡框的两端。

关键人物细节：强调他们绝不是塑料模型；他们拥有清晰可见的皮肤毛孔、自然的头发细节以及极其逼真的布料纹理和褶皱。他们正在享用看起来热气腾腾、新鲜烹饪的符合人物身份的真实食物微缩模型，抬头看向镜头。

微信独有视觉元素：气泡框内部只有文字内容：“[文字内容]”。在气泡框的正上方外部，居中显示一个灰色的微信风格时间戳：“[时间戳]”。

背景细节：整个背景完全被高密度的、无缝连接的定制微信主题线条图案所填满（包含微信标志性的双气泡Logo、朋友圈图标、红包图标、“摇一摇”手势、经典黄脸表情包等线条艺术），从边缘到边缘覆盖整个画面，没有空隙，模仿密集的聊天背景壁纸风格。

技术参数：采用专业演播室级微距布光，强调质感，8K超高分辨率，整个平面焦点极其锐利。
```

### 130. 精确姿态与构图复制提示

**作者**: [骑司Chase](https://x.com/qisi_ai/status/2005190547133399118)  **日期**: 2025-12-28  **语言**: zh

> 一个高度技术性的中文提示，专为图像到图像生成（Nano Banana Pro）设计，严格要求将参考图像的姿势、摄像机角度、构图和取景复制到来自不同源图像的主体上，同时禁止对主体的身份或风格进行任何更改。

![精确姿态与构图复制提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061668708_bwo6di_G9PclW2bgAEDApq.jpg)
![精确姿态与构图复制提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061669070_eco6p8_G9PcmH_bMAA6ifD.jpg)

```
一、核心目标与强约束
1 姿势精确复刻：以图二为姿势唯一参考，将图一人物的全身姿势进行“逐点对齐”复刻（头、颈、肩、胸、髋、膝、踝、手臂、手腕、手指的朝向与弯曲程度一致）。
2 视角与镜头一致：相机机位、拍摄角度、镜头高度、俯仰角、左右偏转角、透视关系、景深效果与图二一致。
3 构图一致：人物在画面中的位置、占比、留白比例、裁切方式（是否截到脚/头顶/手）与图二一致。
4 头部与视线一致：头部倾斜角度、下巴抬/收程度、视线方向与图二一致。
5 外观禁止改动：严格保留图一人物的身份特征与风格（脸型五官、发型发色、肤色、服装款式与颜色、材质、配饰、纹理、体型比例、年龄气质、画风/渲染风格），只改变姿势与镜头构图以匹配图二。

二、执行方式与校准要求
1 对齐方法：以图二人物骨架为“目标骨架”，将图一人物骨架“重定向”到目标骨架；四肢角度、重心位置、躯干扭转幅度必须匹配。
2 关键点优先级：先匹配重心与骨盆朝向，再匹配躯干旋转与肩线，再匹配四肢末端（手、脚），最后微调手指与表情细节。
3 允许变化范围：姿势与镜头的误差尽可能为0；若不可避免，误差必须极小且不可肉眼明显。
4 禁止项：禁止新增或删除物体；禁止改变服装造型与细节；禁止改变人物风格；禁止换背景风格导致构图变化；禁止把图二人物的外观特征迁移到图一人物身上。
```

### 131. 手绣丝绸专辑封面提示（音乐/歌词）

**作者**: [sundyme](https://x.com/sundyme/status/2005129744690675731)  **日期**: 2025-12-28  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的模板提示，用于生成一张超详细的专辑封面，风格为手绣丝绸艺术，包含歌词和音乐元素。它要求可见的、逼真的缝线细节、特定的调色板和排版布局，以呈现精致、考究的美感。

![手绣丝绸专辑封面提示（音乐/歌词）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061783878_ziw62d_G9LqAHxasAAOo20.jpg)

```
Ultra-detailed album cover for \"{argument name="song title" default="歌曲名称"}\". Style: Huang Hai's minimalist aesthetic with HIGH-QUALITY HAND-EMBROIDERED SILK ART. Format: Vertical Poster (1:1 aspect ratio).

CRITICAL: Every element must appear as hand-embroidered with visible, realistic stitching details. Show individual thread stitches, slight texture variations, and authentic embroidery craftsmanship.

Visual Structure: 
- Delicate high-end silk fabric background with subtle sheen and fine weave texture, {argument name="color scheme" default="[配色方案]"}, occupying 75% of canvas.
- Scene Visualization: A simplified, poetic scene of {argument name="scene description" default="[场景描述]"}, rendered in hand-embroidered silk with VISIBLE REALISTIC STITCHING DETAILS.
- Scale Contrast: Tiny, barely visible silhouettes of [细节元素] at the bottom/corners.

Base: Luxurious silk fabric background with subtle sheen, fine weave texture, and soft luminous quality.

HAND-EMBROIDERY DETAILS: Every element must show:
- Individual visible thread stitches with slight texture
- Microscopic silk thread details with subtle metallic sheen
- Realistic embroidery craftsmanship with slightly imperfect, organic stitching
- Visible stitch patterns and thread texture variations
- Authentic hand-embroidered appearance with natural imperfections
The scene features soft muted colors (pale [颜色] for the [元素], muted [颜色] for the [元素], soft [颜色] for the [元素]). Realism: Extreme dimensional depth, realistic hand-embroidered stitches, tactile silk texture with visible stitch details.

Color Palette: Subtle high-end [主色调] silk background. Soft muted colors for the scene (pale [颜色], muted [颜色], soft [颜色]). Elegant, refined, and sophisticated mood.

Typography: 
- Top title \"[歌曲名称]\" in minimalist elegant serif typography (hand-embroidered in subtle thread), surrounded by maximum breathing space.
- Subtitle \"[艺术家] • [年份] • [风格类型]\" in refined font.
- Small bilingual text \"[英文关键词] [中文关键词]\" in refined font.

CRITICAL - BOTTOM DESIGN: The text must show OBVIOUS hand-embroidered style with:
- Spacing between individual stitches visible
- Organic, slightly imperfect stitch patterns
- Natural texture variations in the thread
- Hand-stitched appearance rather than dense machine embroidery
- Clear manual embroidery craftsmanship

Bottom Design: Elegant flow of musical notes intertwined with refined calligraphy showcasing TWO COHESIVE, NARRATIVE-FULL lyrics from the song:
Line 1: \"{argument name="first lyric line" default="[第一句歌词]"}\"\nLine 2: \"{argument name="second lyric line" default="[第二句歌词]"}\"\nRendered in elegant [书法风格] style calligraphy with refined strokes, all hand-embroidered with VISIBLE INDIVIDUAL STITCHES. The text should show clear hand-stitched style with spacing between stitches. [音乐风格] musical notes arranged in subtle [图案] patterns. Embroidered in [主色线] and [辅色线] threads, connecting notes and text with delicate [线条类型] lines, showing OBVIOUS hand-embroidered texture with individual stitch visibility.

Border: Minimal single thin line border in [边框颜色] (hand-embroidered). Corner: One small elegant [符号] symbol (hand-stitched
```

**作者**: [light](https://x.com/Lightdev20/status/2005124403882066291)  **日期**: 2025-12-28  **语言**: en

> 一个高度具体的 JSON 提示，专为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计，旨在生成一张混乱、低保真、独立风潮（Indie Sleaze）美学的图像。画面中，一名年轻女子倒置（头部位于画面底部），身旁有吉他，手里夹着一支香烟，置身于一个杂乱的卧室中。图像强调刺眼的直射闪光、高颗粒感、单色的黄/绿色调，以及一次性胶片相机那种原始、抓拍的视觉效果。

![Indie Sleaze 闪光快照：倒置吉他姿势](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061662600_gtrt6i_G9Oh-IJbQAA2KPm.jpg)

```
{
  "subject_matter": {
      "main_subject": "Young woman with dark curly hair lying supine and inverted (head at bottom of frame), holding a cream-colored electric guitar across her chest, smoking a cigarette.",
      "secondary_elements": "A cluttered, chaotic bedroom background featuring a desk crowded with various liquor bottles, red cups, and cameras; vintage posters plastered on the walls; wooden furniture.",
      "action_pose": "Passive, rebellious relaxation; lying on back with legs elevated (knees bent), head tilted back looking vaguely towards the lens, holding a lit cigarette in mouth."
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "medium": "Flash Photography / Analog Film Snapshot",
      "art_style": "{argument name="art style" default="Indie Sleaze, 90s Grunge, Lo-fi Aesthetic, Candid snapshot"}",
      "camera_angle": "High-angle, top-down perspective, inverted composition (subject orientation flipped)",
      "lens_type": "35mm wide-angle (capturing context of the messy room)",
      "depth_of_field": "Moderate depth of field (f/5.6), keeping the subject sharp while retaining detail in the cluttered background"
    },
    "lighting_and_atmosphere": {
      "lighting_type": "Harsh direct flash mixed with warm tungsten room lighting",
      "direction": "Frontal (flash) causing harsh shadows and specular highlights on skin",
      "mood": "Rebellious, intoxicated, raw, chaotic, nocturnal, 'cool'",
      "time_of_day": "Night / Artificial interior lighting"
    },
    "color_data": {
      "palette": [
        "Sickly Yellow (#C8C846)",
        "Chartreuse Green (#9FA62D)",
        "Shadow Black (#0F0F0F)",
        "Denim Blue (#3E5F73)",
        "Warm Skin Tone (Yellow Cast)"
      ],
      "grading": "Monochromatic yellow/green tint, high contrast, high grain/noise, cross-processed film look"
    }
  },
  "detailed_construct_prompt": "Flash photography in the style of early 2000s Indie Sleaze. A high-angle, inverted shot of a rebellious young woman lying on her back, head positioned at the bottom of the frame. She is holding a cream-colored electric guitar across her chest and smoking a cigarette with a nonchalant, heavy-lidded expression. She has messy dark curly hair, wearing a pale yellow tank top, silver chain necklace, and baggy blue jeans. The environment is a cramped, chaotic bedroom bathed in a sickly, monochromatic yellow and chartreuse light. The background features a desk cluttered with empty liquor bottles, red cups, and film cameras, with band posters on the walls. Shot on a disposable film camera with direct flash, harsh shadows, heavy film grain, lo-fi texture, and a raw, candid atmosphere."
}
```

01. Create a clean presentation-style overview diagram that shows the entire structure at a glance with labeled sections.

03. Create a bold side-by-side comparison slide with clear visual separation and minimal text.

04. Create a before-and-after presentation slide with strong visual contrast and clear labels.

05. Create a three-step breakdown slide that visually explains the process in simple stages.

06. Create a pyramid-style diagram that visually shows hierarchy from bottom to top.

08. Create a clean timeline slide showing progression from past to future.

09. Create a presentation diagram that highlights the most important points using visual emphasis.

11. Create a roadmap-style slide showing a clear path from start to goal.

12. Create a layered diagram that visually stacks concepts in an easy-to-understand way.

13. Create a relationship diagram showing how key elements connect to each other.

14. Create a presentation slide that emphasizes key numbers with bold visual design.

15. Create a final summary slide that cleanly wraps up all key points in one visual.

### 136. 家庭聚会电影场景

**作者**: [Javeriya ✨](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281/status/2004556367160615387)  **日期**: 2025-12-26  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一个电影般真实感的场景：在一个舒适的沿海客厅里，一家人正在聚会，一位年轻女子正在弹奏数码键盘，而一只燕尾服猫则在琴键上行走，画面采用变形镜头模拟和浅景深拍摄。

![家庭聚会电影场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988101580_1vn20o_G9GdYqdaoAAEOW2.jpg)
![家庭聚会电影场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988101536_veskls_G9GdYuKb0AE2bcc.jpg)

```
{
  "scene_description": {
    "setting": "Cozy coastal countryside living room, relaxed family holiday gathering",
    "action": "Young female playing digital keyboard and singing; a tuxedo cat walks on the keys; family members observing and participating.",
    "mood": "Authentic, lived-in, warm but restrained, joyful."
  },
  "subjects": [
    {
      "role": "Protagonist",
      "description": "Young female, long dark wavy hair with soft rim light, natural flushed cheeks.",
      "attire": "{argument name="protagonist attire" default="White sleeveless home dress, pink floral accents, tied ribbon"}.",
      "action": "Seated at keyboard, singing quietly, reacting with a restrained smile."
    },
    {
      "role": "The Cat",
      "description": "Black-and-white tuxedo cat.",
      "action": "Climbing onto keys, pressing random notes."
    },
    {
      "role": "Grandmother",
      "location": "Long sofa in background",
      "action": "Watching calmly with a glass of tea."
    },
    {
      "role": "Mother",
      "location": "Near sofa",
      "action": "Recording on a phone with subtle pride."
    },
    {
      "role": "Father",
      "location": "Beside the keyboard",
      "action": "Leaning against keyboard, singing along with a mug in hand."
    },
    {
      "role": "Infant Brother",
      "location": "Foreground floor",
      "action": "Absorbed in colorful toys."
    }
  ],
  "environment_details": {
    "interior": {
      "flooring": "Wooden parquet, patterned rug",
      "furniture": "Long sofa, digital keyboard with iPad score",
      "decor": "Houseplants, gently moving curtains"
    },
    "exterior_view": {
      "landscape": "Rolling green hills, calm blue sea, white hillside homes",
      "lighting_source": "Wide window, clean golden-hour daylight"
    }
  },
  "technical_specifications": {
    "framing": "Cinematic medium-close, over-the-shoulder (OTS)",
    "lens_emulation": "Anamorphic lens",
    "depth_of_field": "Shallow, soft cinematic depth, bokeh",
    "lighting_effects": "Neutral balance, clean whites, organic grain, restrained bloom, subtle anamorphic flares",
    "color_science": "Natural skin tones, vivid yet controlled saturation, neutral daylight",
    "aspect_ratio": "4:5"
  }
}
```

### 137. 名画变身熟食拼盘

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2004509495507194326)  **日期**: 2025-12-26  **语言**: en

> 一个独特的提示，指示 AI 扮演美食专家和艺术家，用与画作区域相关的熟食食材，完全重现一幅著名的杰作（如《蒙娜丽莎》）。输出是一个 2x2 的网格，展示了原作、食材地图、制作过程和最终的熟食板。

![名画变身熟食拼盘](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988013522_toozz3_G85kRMRXIAEaIHM.jpg)

```
Act as a world class food expert and artist. 

Input A: Masterpiece painting (e.g., {argument name="painting name" default="Mona Lisa"}, Starry Night, The Scream).

 Analyze composition, colors, mood, elements. Pick the right food ingredients relevant to the region that can be used in the painting. 

Goal: Large charcuterie platter replicating the painting using cured meats, cheeses, fruits, nuts, and other ingredients relevant to that region. 
Rules: decide which ingredients should be used for each part, so the painting looks as realistic as possible but is mainly made out of food. 

2x2 grid: Panel 1: Original painting reference; Panel 2: Ingredient map; Panel 3: Overhead build; Panel 4: Final board with wine pairing.
Output: 1 x 1:1 image, rustic gourmet photography.
```

### 139. 未来感新年杂志封面设计提示

**作者**: [いにしえ@AI Creator｜Will Oldgram](https://x.com/old_pgmrs_will/status/2004485448379289965)  **日期**: 2025-12-26  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度结构化提示，旨在生成一张具有新年主题的高端科技视觉杂志封面。它指定了一个复杂的分层构图，包括带有微妙金箔的白色背景、身着和服与西装混合服饰的动态动漫吉祥物，以及用于报头和专题标题的精确排版，所有这些都遵循现代日本平面设计美学。

![未来感新年杂志封面设计提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988123416_db5fu3_G9FcKIXbsAAsv66.jpg)

```
metadata:
title: "Nano Banana Pro - New Year Special 2026 Edition"
model_context: "High-End Japanese Modern Magazine Cover - Tech-Visual Aesthetic"

image_structure:
composition_type: "Magazine Cover Layout with New Year Motif"
visual_flow: "Top Masthead -> Dynamic Character in Kimono-Style Suit -> New Year Slogan -> Technical Details"
layers:
layer_background:
shape: "Full screen background."
color: "Pure White (#FFFFFF)"
texture: "Subtle gold leaf texture or geometric 'Asanoha' (hemp leaf) patterns in faint light grey. A large, stylized red circle (Rising Sun) positioned offset to the left."
lighting: "Sharp studio lighting with golden rim light."

layer_masthead_top:
location: "Top section."
elements:
- type: "Small Top Text"
text: "NEW ERA | CREATIVE REVOLUTION | {argument name="year" default="2026 AD"}"
style: "Spaced-out, gold-colored elegant sans-serif text."
- type: "Main Brand Logo"
text: "NANO BANANA PRO"
style: "Massive, bold, matte black text. The character's hair or katana tip overlaps the letters."
- type: "Special Edition Subtitle"
text: "謹賀新年 - THE ART OF PROMPTING"
style: "Vertical Japanese calligraphy style on the right side, sleek and modern."
layer_character_main:
location: "Center, dynamic silhouette."

content: "Cool, futuristic Japanese Anime Girl (Nano Banana Pro mascot)."
style: "Ultra-detailed 2D anime art with cinematic shading."
details:
subject: "A creative warrior ready for the new year."
appearance:
hair: "Platinum white hair with vibrant banana-yellow highlights."
clothing: "A fusion of a traditional Kimono and a tactical pilot suit. White base with red accents and gold embroidery. Cybernetic 'Obi' (belt) with glowing neon yellow lights."
accessories: "Stylized katana made of translucent yellow glass (energy blade)."
pose: "A sharp 'Iai' pose or a mid-air dash, looking directly at the viewer with confidence. The kimono sleeves create a wide, dramatic flow across the canvas."
layer_foreground_text:
elements:

- type: "Main Feature Title"
text: "N E W  S T A N D A R D"
location: "Lower third, overlapping character's legs."
style: "Large, bold black typography. The text has a 'glitch' effect with gold particles."
- type: "Teaser Text Block (Left)"
location: "Middle Left."
text: "新年、創造性は加速する。\nAIデザインの頂点へ。\n未踏の表現領域を、\nその手に。"
style: "Clean, vertical Japanese text, dark grey for high legibility."
- type: "Footer Info (Bottom Right)"
location: "Bottom Right corner."
content:
header: "CONTENTS"
list:
- "2026 制作フローの革新"
- "黄金比プロンプトの秘匿"
- "AI×和のデザイン美学"
issue_number:
text: "VOL. 026 | NEW YEAR SPECIAL"
style: "Black rectangle with white/gold text, looking like a premium seal."
style_and_tone:

color_palette:

primary: "White, Deep Red, Matte Black"
secondary: "Electric Yellow (Banana), Metallic Gold"
quality_tags:
- "Masterpiece"
- "New Year visual"

**作者**: [Felix_Lyu](https://x.com/BaoguangL37015/status/2004372706117242890)  **日期**: 2025-12-26  **语言**: zh

> 这是一份详细的多步骤工作流程指南，介绍如何在图像到图像模式下使用 Nano Banana（特别是 Nano Banana 2 或 Pro）生成 RPG Maker 像素地图或知识图谱等素材。它强调使用参考图像（如 RM 瓦片或游戏截图）来保持风格一致性，并提供了一个生成黑暗奇幻 RPG 地图的示例提示。

![使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988112563_2iduen_G9D2U4raoAA8F_2.jpg)
![使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988113123_o9tpg0_G9D2U7saAAAufh7.png)
![使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988113223_sxr3g0_G9D2U4rb0AIdIMy.png)
![使用 Nano Banana 为 RPG Maker 像素地图创建图像到图像工作流](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766988114493_muqlip_G9D2U4rb0AgFNy8.jpg)

```
请你以图 1 为底图生成一张用于 RPG Maker 制作的像素地图。对图片细节加以美化，把森林的图块素材和整体风格替换的更具黑暗幻想风格（画风参考《{argument name="参考游戏" default="艾尔登法环"}》/《{argument name="参考游戏2" default="黑暗之魂"}》）。不要将生成的地图放大缩小或拉伸，多余的地方请留出空白。
```

### 142. 通用圣诞美食海报提示词

**作者**: [苍何](https://x.com/canghe/status/2004146437161210299)  **日期**: 2025-12-25  **语言**: zh

> 这是一个多功能提示词，旨在利用 Nano Banana Pro 生成高质量的商业级圣诞美食海报。用户可以轻松替换食物，并自定义文本元素（中式艺术字体、颜色和位置），以创建个性化的、梦幻般的冬季主题视觉效果，并带有柔和的灯光和浅景深。

![通用圣诞美食海报提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940188997_ayn7yu_G9Afp21WYAAs4Wh.jpg)
![通用圣诞美食海报提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940189710_iqivb7_G9AfsKtXsAAPaAx.jpg)
![通用圣诞美食海报提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940191072_ph6wxt_G9AfrHpXoAEVI6g.jpg)

```
一个由【{argument name="食物" default="这里替换掉食物"}】堆叠而成的金字塔形“圣诞树”，点缀着奶油、黄番茄和薄荷叶（可以换其他）。 甜点细节： 【{argument name="食物" default="这里替换掉食物"}】表面撒有细腻的白色糖粉（如同积雪），并装饰有细小的食用金箔。甜点放置在一个透明的水晶圆盘上。 背景氛围： 柔和的浅粉色背景，带有朦胧的暖黄色串灯（Fairy lights）光晕，营造出梦幻、浪漫、甜美的冬日氛围。 光影风格： 极高画质的商业美食摄影，明亮且柔和的自然光，浅景深（背景虚化），色彩清新自然，富有高级感。 文字元素： 图片左侧有竖排的中文艺术字体“【{argument name="自定义文字 1" default="自定义文字"}】，【{argument name="自定义文字 2" default="自定义文字"}】”，字体颜色为【自定义颜色】，旁边还有一行小字“【自定义文字】”。图片右下方有“【自定义文字】”文字，字体为【自定义颜色】(颜色），字体周围加上一些烫金的花纹。所有文字都与整体画面风格融合。
```

**Related**: [[活动海报]]、[[综合设计]]、[[圣诞节]]

### 143. 为头像添加圣诞帽（图像到图像）

**作者**: [katon](https://x.com/hellokaton/status/2003794212266147961)  **日期**: 2025-12-24  **语言**: en

> 一个简单、实用的图像到图像生成提示，专门用于为上传的个人资料图片主体添加一顶传统的圣诞老人帽。该提示强调精确保留原始艺术风格、身份和构图，确保帽子与匹配的光照和阴影自然融合。

![为头像添加圣诞帽（图像到图像）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935985016_no1f9m_G87oN29a0AA3enJ.jpg)
![为头像添加圣诞帽（图像到图像）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766935985209_c3opx4_G87oNogbYAAWvqu.jpg)

```
Using the user-uploaded reference image as the base, add a classic Christmas Santa hat to the subject.

Style match: preserve the original art style exactly (2D/3D/photorealistic/anime/cartoon), keeping identity, facial features, hairstyle, colors, shading, and overall composition unchanged.

Hat design: traditional Santa hat (red felt with subtle fabric texture, white fluffy trim, white pom-pom). Place it naturally on top of the head, aligned to head angle and hairline. Respect perspective, scale, and head shape.

Integration: match the existing lighting, shadows, highlights, linework, and rendering style. Add realistic contact shadows where the hat touches hair/forehead. Do not alter the face, hair, background, clothing, or any other elements.

Output: square (1:1) avatar, crisp and clear at small profile-picture size.
```

**Related**: [[综合3D]]、[[日系动漫]]、[[综合动漫]]

### 145. 游戏/书籍立体模型概念生成器

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2003195839187943881)  **日期**: 2025-12-22  **语言**: en

> 一个系统提示，指示 AI 扮演世界级的视觉艺术家和内容生成器。它的任务是分析游戏或书籍的核心身份，并在一个掏空且符合情境的壳内构建一个高概念的立体模型。该立体模型必须包含来自著名关卡或场景的微缩元素、资产和角色，其灯光和风格应与原始素材相匹配。

![游戏/书籍立体模型概念生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667300869_y08d02_G8vefZ2XUAAldKe.jpg)
![游戏/书籍立体模型概念生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667301935_truabi_G8vefZ6WcAAtzwY.jpg)

```
<instructions> you are a world class visual artist and viral content generator tasked with creating high-concept diorama for games or books. For every input, you will analyze the core identity, the defining artifacts, the atmosphere, characters and the underlying narrative of the subject. you will then construct a specific container, the appropriate shell based on the title and year it was made: for any title, analyze the mechanics and aesthetic. visualize a hollowed-out item. the interior is a diorama of a famous level or scene. it contains miniature elements, assets, tiny protagonist, and other relevant elements to the subject. lighting & style should be appropriate for the title </instructions>
```

### 148. 冬至城市美食艺术海报提示

**作者**: [Dr.D](https://x.com/Dyorzheng/status/2002699009178124686)  **日期**: 2025-12-21  **语言**: zh

> 城市海报提示（推文 2002592082125578427）的修改版本，专为冬至节量身定制。微型城市岛屿现在由一个巨大的、代表该城市最具传统冬至食物（如饺子或汤圆）的形象承载或包裹。场景设置在一个温暖、充满家庭气息的厨房环境中，伴有蒸汽和柔和的灯光，强调了节日、传统的中国文化风格。

![冬至城市美食艺术海报提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489534156_qc7z3n_G8sEBNnXUAAA5Xy.jpg)
![冬至城市美食艺术海报提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489534021_ud4m9f_G8sEAQZXUAAzudy.jpg)
![冬至城市美食艺术海报提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489534147_pmffvt_G8sEAV-XwAAZdPR.jpg)
![冬至城市美食艺术海报提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489535994_koi6e8_G8sECFfXwAA_Kb-.jpg)

```
一张针对【{argument name="城市名称" default="城市名称"}】的城市渲染数字艺术海报，以冬至节气为整体氛围背景。
画面核心主体是一个漂浮的微型岛屿，形状像所选城市并占据画面大部分内容。岛屿的轮廓与城市在地图上的形状相似，无缝融合城市独特的标志性地标、自然景观及文化元素。
微型岛屿整体由该城市在冬至节气中最具代表性的传统美食意象所承载或包裹。具体美食类型仅选择一种，根据城市与地域文化判断，一定要搜索你的知识库或者互联网获取真相，如饺子、汤圆等，不呈现具体餐盘，而是将这一大号的美食的形态、质感与结构转译为岛屿的外壳、地貌或承托结构，使城市仿佛生长在这份大号冬至食物之上。
岛屿置于基于上述传统美食真实而克制的冬至烹饪场景中，例如炉灶、煮锅\蒸屉或汤锅等日常厨房环境，但背景元素以虚化、柔焦方式呈现，仅作为生活气息与烹饪状态的暗示。蒸汽与热气缓慢上升，与冬季暖色光影共同营造安静、温暖、有人间烟火的节气氛围。
电影般的光影、鲜艳但克制的色彩、航拍视角与冬季光线反射效果，建筑数量不宜过多、不宜过于密集。
岛屿内部展现历史与现代的无缝融合：一部分呈现该城市最具代表性的古代历史建筑；另一部分自然过渡为城市的地标建筑与天际线景观，都呈现出基于当下天气情况（务必确认真实天气情况）的状态。
由锅气形成的立体城市汉字名称 3D 文字漂浮于微型岛屿上方，文字如同一个与冬至、美食和城市文化共生的微缩生态装置。
在画面四周与主体周围添加一层具有冬至节日氛围和当地生活气息的信息排版层，整体风格符合中国传统文化
自动检索与【城市名称】相关的基础城市信息及冬至节气信息，简单介绍，文字排版采用不对称、自然分布的方式，分散排列在画面边缘与留白区域，避免严格网格和居中构图。
在画面角落或边缘位置，以地方节气海报或老日历标注的形式呈现城市的地理坐标、别称或建城年份，以及冬至当日的天气与节气提示，作为装饰性信息元素存在。整体排版保持较多留白，但氛围偏向温暖、生活化、有节日感。
文案精炼简洁。
风格要求：
Octane Render, C4D, Isometric City, Micro World, Living Ecosystem, 8k Resolution, DreamWorks style, 3D modeling, delicate, soft light projection
尺寸，竖版9:16
```

### 149. 城市海报数字艺术提示

**作者**: [歸藏(guizang.ai)](https://x.com/op7418/status/2002592082125578427)  **日期**: 2025-12-21  **语言**: zh

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 生成城市数字艺术海报的高度详细提示。核心概念是一个漂浮在云海之上的微型岛屿，其形状如同城市的地图轮廓，融合了地标、文化和自然元素。该提示包含了特定的艺术风格（Octane Render、梦工厂），3D 文本元素，以及一个用于地理数据的详细、极简信息层，从而创造出一种高端、艺术化的城市渲染效果。

![城市海报数字艺术提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489531230_oaju9a_G8qh4rKagAAXsn-.jpg)

```
一张针对 [{argument name="城市名称" default="城市名称"}] 的城市渲染数字艺术海报。

画面核心主体是一个漂浮在白云上方、形状像所选城市的并且占据画面大部分内容的微型岛屿。岛屿的形状与城市在地图上的形状相似，无缝融合城市独特的标志性地标、自然景观及文化元素。加入城市特有的鸟类、电影般的光影、鲜艳色彩、航拍视角和阳光反射效果，建筑不宜太多太密集。

岛屿展现历史与现代的无缝融合。一部分是该城市最具代表性的古代历史建筑；另一部分平滑过渡为城市的地标建筑和天际线景观。

岛屿漂浮浩瀚云海之上。云海采用该城市所在文化圈的传统艺术风格进行表现。

立体城市拼音或英文名的 3D 文字漂浮在微型岛屿的上方，这组文字像一个生态与文化共生的微缩生态装置。

在画面四周和主体周围，叠加一层极简、高雅、具有博物馆展板质感的信息排版层。主要检索相关的城市信息，主要信息使用经典的衬线字体，辅助数据可使用极细的极简无衬线体。在画面的角落，以类似古典地图集或高级杂志扉页的方式排版。用衬线体标注城市的地理坐标、别称或建城年份，以及当前的天气，作为装饰性的背景信息，整体排版留白极多，排版克制、干净、平衡，如同在欣赏一件珍贵的艺术品。

风格要求： Octane Render, C4D, Isometric City, Micro World, Living Ecosystem, 8k Resolution. DreamWorks style, 3D modeling, delicate, soft light projection.
```

Nintendo Switchのプロンプト👇
---
純黒の虚無を背景に、高コントラストな科学スタジオレンダリングで表現されたNintendo Switch本体(携帯モード)。右側面を捉えたこの緊密なプロファイルビューは、偽色熱X線風のアートスタイルを採用。透明な本体ケースとディスプレイガラスを通して、中央のNVIDIA Tegaカスタムプロセッサ、6.2インチ液晶ディスプレイパネル、バッテリーセル、冷却ファンと放熱機構、左右のJoy-Con接続スロット、ゲームカードスロット、基板配線パターンからなる携帯ゲーム機の精密な内部構造が鮮明に浮かび上がり、鮮烈なヒートマップグラデーションで詳細に描かれる。中央やや上部のTegaプロセッサは鮮やかなオレンジ色から黄色で表現され動作時の適度な発熱(55-65°C)を示し、その背面の小型冷却ファンは青緑色の効率的な冷却効果を、本体下部の大容量リチウムイオンバッテリー(4310mAh)は均一な深い青色から青緑色の安全動作温度(20-30°C)を、6.2インチディスプレイパネルは緑から黄緑色の軽微なバックライト熱(35-40°C)を、左右のJoy-Con接続レール部分は淡い青色の低温状態を、上部のゲームカードスロットは濃い青色の未使用状態を表現。色調は深い冷たい青(バッテリー冷却エリア)から強烈な黄色、オレンジのハイライト(Tegaプロセッサ)へと移行し、正投影法による未来的で臨床的な外観と、柔らかなネオンのような輝きを創出している。携帯性を実現する省電力設計と効率的な熱管理システムが、コンパクトな筐体内に精密に配置され、ヒートパイプによる熱伝導経路、空気の流れを示す青い矢印、基板上の電子部品配置まで視認できる。左右対称に配置されたJoy-Con接続機構の精密さと、本体中央に集約された処理系統の美しい設計が際立つ。

TEXT: "THERMAL X-RAY / ORTHOGRAPHIC VIEW / NINTENDO SWITCH HANDHELD MODE / TEGA CHIP TEMP: 58°C / BATTERY TEMP: 25°C"
```

**Related**: [[数据可视化]]、[[JSON结构化提示]]

### 163. 超逼真 3D 模拟提示词：融化的沙漏

**作者**: [Maki@Sunwood AI Labs.](https://x.com/hAru_mAki_ch/status/1999057700790178235)  **日期**: 2025-12-11  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细系统提示，指示其扮演超现实 3D 艺术家（虚幻引擎 5 风格）。该提示定义了一种结构，用于生成一个充满内容的透明物体图像，模拟折射等物理现象。此特定命令生成了一个古董沙漏玻璃雕塑的图像，它被熔化和扭曲，内部充满像液态金属一样流动的沙子、生锈的小齿轮，以及时间倒流的景象，背景是沙漠日落，带有温暖的橙色和紫色渐变。

![超逼真 3D 模拟提示词：融化的沙漏](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967784896_5ez9w7_G74URvDbEAAWxcb.jpg)

```
あなたは「超現実的な物理シミュレーション」を行う3Dアーティストです。
以下の【構文ルール】と【スタイル】に基づき、入力された【パラメータ】を使用して画像を生成してください。

▼ 1. 生成プロセスと構文ルール (System Logic & Syntax)
Nano Banana Proは、入力された変数を以下の構文（Prompt Structure）に代入して描画を実行すること。

* **構文 (Prompt Structure)**:
    "A transparent **[OBJECT]** filled with **[CONTENT]**. The liquid conforms to the object's shape."
* **物理演算 (Physics)**:
    [CONTENT]（中身）は [OBJECT]（外殻）の境界線内に完全に留まり、ガラスの厚みによる光の屈折（Refraction）をシミュレートする。
* **背景処理 (Background)**:
    Set against a **[BACKGROUND]** backdrop.

▼ 2. デザイン・スタイル指定 (Fixed Style)
* **画風**: Hyper-realistic 3D render (Unreal Engine 5 style)
* **構成**: Minimal aesthetic, Elegant and surreal composition
* **照明**: Soft lighting and reflections, Volumetric glow
* **補足**: Whimsical design elements

▼ 3. 入力テキスト (Final Command)
[OBJECT] = {argument name="オブジェクト" default="溶けかけて歪んだアンティークな砂時計のガラス彫刻"}
[CONTENT] = {argument name="中身" default="液体金属のように流れる砂、錆びた小さな歯車、逆流する時間"}
[BACKGROUND] = {argument name="背景" default="砂漠の夕暮れ、温かみのあるオレンジと紫のグラデーション"}
```

**Related**: [[3D渲染]]、[[综合3D]]、[[超现实]]

### 171. 哥特式点画艺术诗歌可视化

**作者**: [Emily](https://x.com/IamEmily2050/status/1998319980647964689)  **日期**: 2025-12-09  **语言**: en

> 一个创意提示，它以一首短诗为基础生成图像，指定点画艺术风格、点彩渲染、黑白雕刻，以及高对比度的哥特式氛围。

![哥特式点画艺术诗歌可视化](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440068813_4m58ye_G7t1avra8AAsrfV.jpg)
![哥特式点画艺术诗歌可视化](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440070145_tdhsaj_G7t1avnboAAkD_4.jpg)
![哥特式点画艺术诗歌可视化](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440070904_ie7tgz_G7t1avnaoAAaIg2.jpg)
![哥特式点画艺术诗歌可视化](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440070991_zoc8oy_G7t1avoasAAxaXu.jpg)

```
Beneath the silver sickle's silent gleam,
Where every shadow is a dotted grain,
She stands amidst the monochrome dream,
Upon the path of scattered charcoal rain.
The towering pines act as her silent loom,
Weaving the starlight into solid stone,
A solitary figure in the gloom,
Crafting bright jewels where only dark is sown.
Her hands, unseen, thread nebulae to earth,
Giving the countless specks a brilliant birth.

Stipple art style, Pointillism render, Black and white engraving, Atmospheric gothic, High contrast, Mystical, Textured paper.
```

![瓦楞纸艺术作品框格展示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765086551998_hpiq9a_G7fcWg6bYAE9Ksi)
![瓦楞纸艺术作品框格展示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765086553283_0i0rw4_G7fcoPTaYAAuarU)

```
这是一张标准手工艺术品的照片。整体材质：瓦楞纸。 整体颜色：浅棕色（常见瓦楞纸的本色）。 艺术品所展示的内容：它是用瓦楞纸制作的3×4的分隔式大盒子。其中，每个格子里面都展示着（竖直摆放）使用瓦楞纸制作的各种不同职业的工具或用品(物品不能重复，不能超出格子)。它们的制作非常精良，细节都极为丰富，都符合结构学。照片的光照很均匀，亮度适中，每一处的瓦楞纸材质和纹理都非常清晰。
以下为物品列表，总计 12 个，用逗号分隔：
{argument name="物品列表" default="医生包与听诊器、刀具套装与锅、建筑图纸与三角尺、锤子与木工刨、相机与三脚架、工具箱与扳手、画架与调色板、打字机与墨水瓶、缝纫机、园艺工具（铲子与水壶）、显微镜与化学器皿、小提琴与琴弓" }
```

### 178. 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的法线贴图和深度贴图生成提示

**作者**: [Takuma Hashimoto](https://x.com/tkm_hmng8/status/1996037744305570235)  **日期**: 2025-12-03  **语言**: en

> 以下是 Nano Banana Pro 的两个英文提示，用于从输入艺术作品图像生成切线空间法线贴图和物理上合理的深度贴图，适用于通过 WebGL 或 Three.js 进行 3D 风格查看。

![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的法线贴图和深度贴图生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909246223_oejk2i_N_VRX8gtYM5vdGZ-.jpg)

```
Generate a surface normal map from the input artwork image.

Output one RGB image where each pixel encodes the surface normal direction in standard tangent-space format:
•R = X direction
•G = Y direction
•B = Z direction

Requirements:
•Maintain the same resolution and aspect ratio as the input image.
•Normal directions must follow the local geometry implied by brush strokes, shading, and contours.
•Do NOT add new artistic elements or repaint the scene.
•Only infer plausible micro-geometry and surface orientation.
•Ensure smooth, consistent normal transitions without noise.

Generate a depth map from the input artwork image.

Output a single grayscale depth map where:
•White = near to the viewer
•Black = far from the viewer

Requirements:
•Maintain the same resolution and aspect ratio as the input image.
•Depth must be smooth, continuous, and physically plausible.
•Infer only geometric depth that could reasonably exist in the original artwork.
•Do NOT add new objects or details.
•Do NOT stylize, repaint, or reinterpret the scene.
•Avoid texture noise; focus solely on depth structure.
```

**Related**: [[综合3D]]、[[地图]]

---

### 182. 带画框和对话气泡的高细节故事艺术布局

**作者**: [かし子🍩](https://x.com/Kashiko_AIart/status/1991801500096446888)  **日期**: 2025-11-21  **语言**: ja

> 一个可以替代“漫画”的词，它描述了一种三格高分辨率的故事艺术布局，其中包含精细的角色、全彩背景和对话气泡，模仿了艺术书籍的风格。

![带画框和对话气泡的高细节故事艺术布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886568939_6pwyg4_G6RB7o1bQAA-rYr.jpg)
![带画框和对话气泡的高细节故事艺术布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886581093_d9bi8b_G6RB86zaAAAkYmc.jpg)

```
構図：{argument name="フレーム数" default="3"}つのフレームに分割された「高精細ストーリーアート」。

背景はフルカラーの背景美術品質。  
キャラクターは高密度のディテール描写。吹き出しでキャラクターのセリフを表現する。  
全体は画集のような高級感のある“アートレイアウト”で構成されている。
参考画像の画風を忠実に再現し、繊細な線画・高精細に仕上げてください。
```

### 189. 三项高级抽象推理图像测试

**作者**: [空心极](https://x.com/MEW201703/status/1991564819284242550)  **日期**: 2025-11-20  **语言**: zh

> 这条推文包含三个独立的详细提示：一个粉笔手写的二次方程推导，一个超现实的金色潘洛斯三角，以及一个类似回文构词法的 LIFE/DEATH 设计，每个都测试了视觉推理的不同方面。

![三项高级抽象推理图像测试](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886723598_6lupjh_G6N1o9faoAAGufy.jpg)
![三项高级抽象推理图像测试](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886726447_frdz7f_G6N1o9iacAEU-4-.jpg)
![三项高级抽象推理图像测试](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886728911_y6001a_G6N1o9gacAQFHES.jpg)
![三项高级抽象推理图像测试](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886731878_8p94bz_G6N1o93awAAT-xX.jpg)

```
一张绿色黑板的特写照片。用白色粉笔写着一元二次方程求根公式的正确推导步骤。第一行：ax^2 + bx + c = 0。第二行：x^2 + (b/a)x = -c/a。第三行：配方。最后一行：x = \frac{-b \pm \sqrt{b^2 - 4ac}}{2a}。字迹工整清晰。不要乱码。

一张用抛光黄金制成的彭罗斯三角的超写实照片，放在大理石桌子上。这个物体形成了一个连续的、不可能的三角形视错觉。几何结构没有断裂。摄影棚布光。

一个双向图的平面设计艺术。正着看单词是'LIFE'，旋转180度倒过来看单词是'DEATH'。白纸黑墨，哥特书法风格。
```

**Related**: [[综合设计]]、[[超现实]]
